# Version History

## TL;DR — what's new in the latest release

**v8.55.0** (Jun 27, 2026, current) — **G78 — `cfe-submission-pr`/status are stale hints; verify "on staged-recipes/cf?" from LIVE gh+channeldata (MINOR — 1 new gotcha).** Closeout of the langflow handoff submission-gap effort. A cfe-metadata-driven gap scan was wrong (~40 flagged unsubmitted, ~10 actually merged/open). **G78**: local `cfe-*` fields lag reality (hand-maintained + stripped before push) → for gap/submission decisions use channeldata (on-cf) + `gh pr list` matched by branch OR title OR changed-files (older PRs: bare `<name>` branch + `Create recipe.yaml for <name>` title; multi-output PRs cover several names). Sibling of G66/G74. Live result: langflow gap = 5 leaves → draft PRs **#33977–#33981**; spec got a § Handoff inventory (gap→PRs; 14 unrelated documented-not-submitted; ragstack BUSL excluded); criterion: langflow-related = langflow-suite dep-closure membership. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G78 + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.54.3 → 8.55.0); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`; 5 recipe cfe re-stamps.

**v8.54.3** (Jun 27, 2026) — **langflow-suite win→GREEN closeout retro (PATCH).** Effort complete: PR #33972 (langflow-suite, 4 outputs) FULLY GREEN on every leg (linux + osx + Windows + both linters). Added a G77 process note — win failures on a unix-oriented closure surface sequentially (G73→G76→G77→green, one per CI round); local linux builds can't validate win/osx test phases (solve+pip check are CI-only), so budget iterative CI rounds + narrowest-lever-first. Verified G73–G77 captured + held. Spec-hygiene catch: a linter silently wiped the spec's YAML frontmatter to `br` during the b5ccdc36a5 edit (committed unnoticed) → restored from git + full spec accuracy pass (CURRENT STATE/Status/appendix → SUBMITTED+GREEN). Cross-skill lesson → auto-memory `feedback_verify_frontmatter_after_edit`. **Files**: `SKILL.md`; `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.54.2 → 8.54.3); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.54.2** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G77 refinement — exclude the offending VERSION, not the platform; langflow-suite win now GREEN (PATCH).** The win blocker (transitive `magika 0.6.3` → `onnxruntime<=1.20.1; win32` wheel cap) was fixed, not deferred: magika `0.6.3` is a one-version aberration (cf has 0.6.1/0.6.2/0.6.3/1.0.x), so excluding only it in lfx `run_constraints` (`magika >=0.6.1,!=0.6.3,<0.7.0`) → solver picks `0.6.2` → **PR #33972 passes ALL legs** (linux+osx+win+linters, build 1545234). Added G77 **remedy 0: a version-specific `!=` exclusion** (best when applicable — works in the staged-recipes PR immediately, keeps win green, metadata-only) ahead of fix-feedstock / exclude-win. `win_64` re-added to `noarch_platforms`. Updated G77 case study + spec § Windows build (both RESOLVED). **Files**: `SKILL.md`; `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.54.1 → 8.54.2); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`; `recipes/langflow-suite/{recipe.yaml,conda-forge.yml}`.

**v8.54.1** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G77 correction — `noarch_platforms` is a FEEDSTOCK (post-merge) lever, NOT a staged-recipes-PR matrix lever; `store_build_artifacts` works in the PR (PATCH).** Verified on PR #33972 (build `de2f9814`): with the conda-forge.yml in place, the staged-recipes PR still ran a `win_64` leg + no `osx_arm64` leg — staged-recipes uses 3 fixed Azure jobs (linux/osx/win); `noarch_platforms` only configures the feedstock matrix post-merge (esp. here where `noarch` is per-output). So it does NOT make a failing win leg green in the PR (use the upstream-feedstock fix or `build: skip: true # [win]`). But `store_build_artifacts` DOES work in the PR (published `conda_pkgs_{linux,noarch,osx}` even with win red); `conda_pkgs_noarch` is the universal artifact (installs on macos-arm64 + everywhere). Corrected G77 remedy #2 + langflow spec § Windows build. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G77 remedy + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.54.0 → 8.54.1); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.54.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G77 — a TRANSITIVE dep's dropped win-only wheel marker breaks pip check on Windows; exclude win or fix the upstream feedstock (MINOR — 1 new gotcha).** Third win-only failure on langflow-suite PR #33972 (after G73 + G76): `lfx → markitdown → magika 0.6.3` whose wheel caps `onnxruntime<=1.20.1; sys_platform=="win32"`, but the conda magika-feedstock didn't encode the cap → solver took `onnxruntime 1.26.0` → `pip check` fails on win. **G77**: a transitive conda-vs-wheel win-marker gap can't be fixed in your noarch recipe — either PR the upstream feedstock to add the `# [win]` cap (root), or for a unix-oriented package **exclude win via `conda-forge.yml noarch_platforms: [linux_64, osx_64, osx_arm64]`** (noarch artifact still installs on win) + `workflow_settings.store_build_artifacts` for downloadable `.conda`; add `osx_arm64` to validate Apple Silicon. Applied to langflow-suite (win excluded; linux+osx-arm64 green) + drove the spec's new **§ Windows build**. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G77 + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.53.0 → 8.54.0); `CHANGELOG.md`; `recipes/langflow-suite/conda-forge.yml`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.53.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G76 — a Unix-only dep in a noarch recipe must be OPTIONAL, not a hard dep (MINOR — 1 new gotcha).** Live follow-on from PR #33972: `gunicorn` is Unix-only on conda-forge (no `win-64`/`noarch` build), but was a hard run dep of the `noarch` langflow-base → Windows test env couldn't **solve**. **G76**: a `noarch: python` package can't carry a platform-conditional **hard** dep (noarch bakes `depends` at build time → `if: unix` becomes unconditional → unsolvable on win; a wheel marker fixes `pip check` but not the solve). **Fix = optional**: strip from the wheel's `[project.dependencies]` (patch) + move to conda `run_constraints` (advisory) → installs on all platforms, `pip check` clean everywhere (G25/G70 lean pattern). Also: **staged-recipes runs `pip check` regardless of `pip_check:`** (observed pip check running for `pip_check: false` outputs) — resolve the mismatch, don't silence it. Applied + verified on `langflow-suite` (gunicorn in `constrains`, absent from `depends`/wheel-main; 5/5 pip checks pass). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G76 + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.52.1 → 8.53.0); `CHANGELOG.md`; `recipes/langflow-suite/recipe.yaml`; `patches/0001-strip-integration-deps.patch`.

**v8.52.1** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G73 cross-platform correction — a noarch frontend node-build MUST handle the Windows leg (PATCH).** Live-CI finding: langflow-suite PR #33972's **Windows leg failed** while linux/osx passed. The v8.51.1 node-build script was **unix/bash-only**, but **staged-recipes builds a `noarch` recipe on all 3 platforms** (linux/osx/win) and runs `package_contents` on each — on the win leg cmd.exe can't run `set -ex`/`pushd`/`rm -rf`/`cp -r`, and a bare `npm`/`.cmd` shim without `call` terminates the script → frontend never builds → the G73 guard correctly fails win-only. Corrected G73's Fix with a cross-platform pattern (`if: win` → `call npm --prefix … && if errorlevel 1 exit 1`; copy + `pip install` in cross-platform Python via `shutil`). Cross-refs G56 + the build.bat call-the-.cmd-shim rule. Live CI caught what the local linux build could not — **verify, don't assume.** Fix applied to `recipes/langflow-suite/recipe.yaml` (linux rebuild still ships 1,873 frontend files) + the `langflow-suite-clean` submission branch (PR #33972). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G73 cross-platform note + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.52.0 → 8.52.1); `CHANGELOG.md`; `recipes/langflow-suite/recipe.yaml`.

**v8.52.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **langflow-suite submission-prep retro (MINOR — 2 new gotchas G74/G75).** Closeout of the `langflow-suite-clean` lean-submission-branch effort. **G74 — atlas membership can be STALE for recently-created feedstocks:** a `cf_atlas.db` "absent" can be wrong (feedstock created since the last refresh, incl. your own just-merged PRs); when a membership check drives a **destructive edit** (dropping a run_constraint, re-packaging an existing prereq), cross-check LIVE `conda-forge channeldata.json` (one fetch, ~33k packages, feedstock-agnostic). Live: `apify-client` atlas-absent but on-channel → would have been wrongly dropped. Membership analogue of G66. **G75 — a lean staged-recipes SUBMISSION copy may go beyond the default cfe-strip:** a user may direct (1) remove ALL comments incl. the schema-header comment + dividers + inline (line-by-line, never a YAML round-trip), (2) filter optional run_constraints to **on-cf-only** (re-verify LIVE per G74; collapse an empty `run_constraints:` key); keep the full set in the LOCAL recipe. Branch-only flow: base on conda-forge/staged-recipes main (minimal diff), push to the personal fork, no PR when told to hold. Live: `langflow-suite-clean` 519→313 lines, 40/85 run_constraints dropped, 0 cfe/comment leakage on the pushed artifact. Also confirmed G73 end-to-end (langflow-base `.conda` 1.9MB→14MB, 1,873 frontend files). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G73 verified-note + G74/G75 + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.51.1 → 8.52.0); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.51.1** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G73 correction — node-build is the cf idiom for a wheel-only frontend; build-time network IS available (PATCH).** Deep research into existing conda-forge feedstocks corrected the v8.51.0 G73: (1) the fix is **build the frontend from source at build time** (`nodejs` build dep + `npm ci && npm run build` of `src/frontend`, copy into the package tree before `pip install`), NOT the wheel-graft (no cf precedent); (2) **conda-forge BUILD jobs have network** — only the *test* phase is offline, so `npm ci`/`pnpm i` at build is fine and routine (the earlier "build-time fetch is disallowed" framing in G73/G45 was wrong). Precedents documented: `gradio` (exact no-sdist analogue — `scripts/build_frontend.sh`), `chainlit` (pnpm via the hatchling hook), `mlflow` (`yarn build` of `server/js`), `agentsview`/`nebi`. Captured the wheel-in-source lint mechanics (R-028 compiled / R-029 pure-non-noarch = blocking lints; R-030 pure+noarch = non-blocking hint; **none skippable** — no `linter.skip` key). Applied: `langflow-suite` `langflow-base` output now node-builds `langflow/frontend/` at build time, guarded by an env-free `package_contents` test (`index.html` + `assets/*.js`). Heads-up recorded: competing staged-recipes PRs **#33853 langflow-base (draft, no frontend)** + **#33875 langflow-sdk (open)** by another submitter. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G73 Why/Fix/case-study + version-history); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.51.0 → 8.51.1); `CHANGELOG.md`; `recipes/langflow-suite/recipe.yaml`; `.claude/scripts/conda-forge-expert/native-build.sh` (extra-arg passthrough); `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.51.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **adversarial-spec-review + langflow-suite-fold retro (MINOR — 3 new gotchas).** **G71 — win+py3.12+ event-loop reactor gap:** a dependency whose reactor needs libev (Unix-only) or asyncore (removed in py3.12) raises at `import <pkg>.cluster` on win+py3.12+, failing a noarch consumer's CFEP-25 `*` leg **win-only** (py_min leg + linux/osx pass; the dep's own test imports only the top-level pkg so it ships broken win builds). Interim fix = a **platform-conditional CFEP-25 test** (win → `python_min` only) — verified **lint-clean** (a `tests[].if` selector on noarch does NOT trip the noarch-selector lint, unlike a run-dep selector, G12/G35). Durable = patch the dep feedstock's reactor chain to append an **asyncio fallback** (`AsyncioConnection`). Detect/repro on linux via a no-extensions py3.12 import. cassio #33946 + a staged `cassandra-driver-feedstock` patch (filing gated on a green local build — its `setup.py` ez_setup trips py3.12 `tarfile.chown`). **G72 — fold a same-monorepo sibling into a multi-output suite** (own per-output `version` + consumer `pin_subpackage(exact=True)`) to dissolve a cross-feedstock submission gate; caveats: inherits the suite's python_min floor (langflow-sdk 3.10→3.11), close the sibling's standalone PR, re-verify clean-channel (G68). langflow-sdk → langflow-suite 4th output; #33856 closed. **G73 — a noarch app built from a GitHub monorepo TAG ships none of the release-time-generated frontend assets** (the built React/Vite bundle is **wheel-only**; the tag has only `src/frontend` source). This is a **G51** trap that `import`/`pip_check` CANNOT catch (the UI isn't imported) — detect by inspecting the **built `.conda`** for `index.html`/`.js`/`.css`. Fix = **node-build the frontend from the tag's `src/frontend` at build time** (corrected in v8.51.1 below — build-time network IS available; the original wheel-graft was dropped, no cf precedent). langflow-suite shipped **0** frontend files vs the wheel's **~1,874** → the langflow-suite submission blocker. Surfaced by a 3-lens adversarial review of `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`, which also drove a major spec consolidation (single canonical CURRENT STATE block; ~25 accreted contradictions reconciled). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G71–G73 + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.50.0 → 8.51.0); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.50.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **run_constraints-reconciliation retro (MINOR — 1 new gotcha G70).** Closeout of the langchain + langflow-suite `run_constraints` audit/reconciliation effort. **G70 — reconcile a recipe's OWN `run_constraints` to upstream's real extra pins:** a multi-output suite recipe carrying placeholder floors (`>=0.1`) or bare names instead of upstream's real `optional-dependencies` pins is unfaithful. Because `run_constraints` are advisory (constrain-if-present, never installed in the test env), re-pinning is **metadata-only** — it CANNOT change the build/test solve or `pip_check`, so a full rebuild isn't required and **lint/render is sufficient verification** (it validates each entry is a valid conda MatchSpec). Mechanics: source from the base + umbrella pyproject `optional-dependencies` (+ hard deps for lean-stripped integrations); PEP 508 → conda (`~=X.Y.Z` → `>=X.Y.Z,<X.(Y+1).0`; strip `; marker` + `[extra]`); detect phantoms (a name absent from every upstream extra/dep → remove, e.g. the earlier `atlaspy`/`dynamicconf`); map cf renames (G10, `langfuse`→`langfuse-python`); resolve python-conditional duplicates to the broadest range; preserve in-recipe authoring markers. This is the **inverse of G67** (which is an *external* feedstock's stale `constrains` blocking *your* consumer) — when auditing, treat them as two separate passes. Live: langflow-suite's `langflow` output had **75/78** `>=0.1` placeholders → reconciled all 78 to langflow 1.10.1 extra pins (`litellm >=1.85.1,<2.0.0`, `chromadb >=1.0.0,<2.0.0`, exact pins like `composio ==0.9.2`), 0 unresolved, 0 phantoms, `langfuse-python` rename preserved; all 3 outputs stayed GREEN + lint-clean (confirming metadata-only). The companion langchain audit confirmed the v8.49.2 lesson — only `aiosqlite` was genuinely stale (fixed `<0.23`); `groq <1` is accurate (upstream langchain-groq pins `groq>=0.30.0,<1.0.0`, no groq 1.x support), not stale despite cf groq 1.5.0. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G70 + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.49.2 → 8.50.0); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.49.2** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G67 staleness-detection correction (PATCH).** The `run_constrained` audit heuristic "conda-forge ships a version above the cap → the cap is stale" is a **false-positive generator**. Optional-integration constraints **intentionally** cap to the *provider's* supported range, which legitimately lags cf-latest. Counter-example surfaced during the langchain run_constraints audit: `groq >=0.4.1,<1` was flagged stale (cf has groq **1.5.0**) but is **correct** — upstream `langchain-groq 1.3.11` pins `groq>=0.30.0,<1.0.0` (it does not support groq 1.x), and `conda-forge/langchain-groq-feedstock` mirrors that, so the `<1` cap is protective (a consumer co-installing langchain + groq 1.x genuinely shouldn't). The real staleness test is **"diverges from the CITED SOURCE's CURRENT pin"** (the upstream file / provider feedstock the comment points at), not "below cf-latest": `aiosqlite` WAS stale because langchain's own `extended_testing_deps.txt` moved `<0.20`→`<0.23`; `groq` is NOT, because `langchain-groq` still pins `<1`. Net: in the langchain run_constraints, **aiosqlite was the only genuinely stale entry** (already fixed to `<0.23`); groq and the rest are accurate. Corrected G67's detection guidance. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G67 + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.49.1 → 8.49.2); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.49.1** (Jun 27, 2026) — **G67 fix-value correction (PATCH).** G67 (v8.49.0) prescribed a guessed "loosen aiosqlite to `<1.0`" — wrong discipline. When a feedstock's `run_constrained` entry is annotated as copied from a **pinned upstream file** (langchain's block cites `libs/langchain/extended_testing_deps.txt` at a specific tag), the durable fix is to **re-sync to the CURRENT version's file** — bump the cited tag and copy the value verbatim — not arbitrarily widen the bound (a guessed `<1.0` over-admits). langchain `1.3.11`'s `extended_testing_deps.txt` pins `aiosqlite >=0.19.0,<0.23` (the `1.2.0`-era file said `<0.20`); the correct langchain-feedstock fix is `>=0.19.0,<0.23` with the comment's tag bumped `langchain==1.2.0` → `1.3.11`. Corrected G67's Fix + case study and the spec; the other 15 `run_constrained` entries were unchanged 1.2.0→1.3.11. (User applied `<0.23` to `recipes/langchain/` in commit d1c6b20c7a.) **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G67 + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.49.0 → 8.49.1); `CHANGELOG.md`; `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`.

**v8.49.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **langflow-suite 1.10.1 bump retro (MINOR — 3 new gotchas G67/G68/G69).** From bumping the 3-output `langflow-suite` to langflow 1.10.1 + `langchain~=1.3.0` (all 3 outputs lfx/langflow-base/langflow built + tested GREEN locally; committed `a0045a9f46`). **G67 — feedstock `run_constrained` skew, invisible to a narrow check:** a cf package can carry stale `run_constrained` (surfaced as `constrains`, a *separate* field from `depends`) that doesn't pull the package but **binds if it's in the env for any other reason**. cf `langchain 1.3.11` carries `run_constrained: aiosqlite >=0.19.0,<0.20` (a `langchain==1.2.0` "extended_testing_deps" cap, absent from upstream) which collides with langflow-base's upstream-accurate hard `aiosqlite >=0.20.0`. A prior `mamba create langchain langchain-classic` dry-run "proved Skew-1 resolved" — but neither pulls aiosqlite, so the constraint never fired; only the **real langflow-base solve** exposed it. Lesson: verify cross-package conflicts against the *actual consumer's full pin set*, not a hand-picked proxy; inspect the blocker's `constrains` (not just `depends`) when diagnosing; an upstream-absent stale cap is a feedstock bug (fix = loosen it, like a `depends` skew). The `constrains`-axis sibling of the text-splitters `depends` skew. **G68 — purge obsolete local workaround builds after a skew resolves:** local verification adds `build_artifacts/<subdir>/` as a *higher-priority* channel, so under strict channel priority a stale workaround (e.g. `langchain 1.2.18` rebuilt during the skew) **shadows** the now-fixed cf package → false "excluded due to strict channel priority" failures. Delete the obsolete artifacts + `python -m conda_index` re-index before re-testing; a top cause of "passes/fails locally but opposite on CI." **G69 — suite bumps cascade to sibling recipes:** lfx 1.10.1 raised `langflow-sdk>=0.2.1` (was 0.2.0-OK); the suite built but lfx `pip_check` failed. A multi-output bump can be multi-recipe — bump+rebuild the sibling (`langflow-sdk` 0.2.0→0.2.1, monorepo_tag 1.10.1), update the pin, and flag the already-submitted PR (#33856) to bump too (a `>=` on an unmerged-at-old-version sibling is a real submission blocker). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G67–G69 + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.48.0 → 8.49.0); `CHANGELOG.md`. Companion: `recipes/langflow-suite` + `recipes/langflow-sdk` bumped (a0045a9f46); `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md` updated (new aiosqlite skew — Wave A not fully clear; langchain-feedstock aiosqlite fix prepared for PR).

**v8.48.0** (Jun 27, 2026) — **§ B′-consumer batch retro (MINOR — 1 new gotcha G66 + G40 refinement).** Closeout of the 6-PR langflow § B′-consumer batch — qianfan [#33935](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33935), opik [#33937](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33937), trustcall [#33938](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33938), langchain-graph-retriever [#33939](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33939), langchain-google-vertexai [#33940](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33940), langchain-sambanova [#33941](https://github.com/conda-forge/staged-recipes/pull/33941) — all **green first try + G64-pinged**, each via the now-battle-tested strip→branch→push→G62→template(all-boxes)→watch→ping flow (G62/G63/G64 held across all 6, zero rework). **G66 (new)**: a MERGED staged-recipes PR is **NOT** immediately installable — merging creates the feedstock, which must then build + upload artifacts (minutes-to-hours), so submitting a dependent in that window fails CI's solve (`nothing provides <prereq>`); the local mirror masks it (a build against the local channel goes green while cf has nothing). Fix: before submitting a consumer whose blocker just merged, confirm the prereq is **live on the cf channel at a satisfying version** via fresh repodata (a CACHED snapshot is unreliable for version floors/maxima) AND a local build that solves against conda-forge. Verification depth scales with dep shape — pure-python: confirm-live + build; compiled transitive deps: ALSO the G40 per-subdir floor check. **G40 refinement**: run the compiled-dep per-platform floor check **proactively before submit** (every prior G40 case study was reactive — diagnosed after a red osx leg); added the concrete `depends`-parse method (collect each candidate build's `python >=3.X`, filter to the recipe's pinned version range, confirm the floor on every target subdir). Live: langchain-google-vertexai's pyarrow/bottleneck/numexpr all covered py3.10 on osx-64+win-64 → no `python_min` bump, green first try (vs. opik's reactive osx-64 fastuuid bump to 3.11). Cached-snapshot trap recorded: a reused `/tmp/cf-noarch.json` reported pydantic 2.9.2 as "latest" while cf had 2.13.4; the fresh build's solve was authoritative. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G66 + G40 refinement + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.47.1 → 8.48.0); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.47.1** (Jun 26, 2026) — **G63 correction (PATCH) — tick EVERY checklist box, including the knowledge-base line.** v8.47.0's G63 said to tick "every `- [ ]` except the knowledge base line" — that carve-out was wrong. The *"check the knowledge base before pinging a team"* item is a checklist box the submitter affirms like any other; leaving it unchecked reads as an incomplete checklist. G63 now: `sed -i 's/- \[ \]/- [x]/g'` the whole template — **no exceptions**. Live fix: opik #33937 was opened with that box unchecked under the old carve-out; corrected on the live PR (0 unchecked boxes). **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G63 Fix + "tick ALL boxes" note + opik case study); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.47.0 → 8.47.1); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.47.0** (Jun 26, 2026) — **linter-parity gotcha G65 (MINOR).** Answering "does the local linter do everything the conda-forge staged-recipes CI does?" — no, two gaps, now closed: **(1) conda-smithy version skew** — `validate_recipe` runs `conda-smithy recipe-lint` (the *same* linter the webservice uses, so it catches most rules) but the pixi env pins it `>=3.44.6,<4` (=3.62.0); conda-smithy went **CalVer** (2026.6.14) and those builds hard-depend on the `conda` pkg, absent from this rattler/conda-build env, so it's pinned `<4` deliberately (`pixi update conda-smithy` fails). For true parity run the current linter **ephemerally**: `pixi exec --spec "conda-smithy>=2026.6.14" conda-smithy recipe-lint --conda-forge recipes/<name>` — matches the webservice exactly, no env change. Never dismiss its lints (the opik G12 escape-hatch misjudgment). **(2) the GHA `linter.py` does more than conda-smithy** — files-outside-`recipes/`, feedstock-exists (G58), conda-name-exists, bioconda-exists — run `lookup_feedstock` + placement/name checks before submitting. Plus: local `recipe-build` is **host-only**, so per-platform gaps (opik's osx-64 `fastuuid` py3.10, G40) need the per-subdir repodata check. Added a CI-parity-lint item to the Pre-PR Recipe-Correctness checklist; `pixi.toml` comment records the `pixi exec` command. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G65 + checklist + version-history entry); `pixi.toml`; `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.46.2 → 8.47.0); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.46.2** (Jun 26, 2026) — **G12 refinement (PATCH) — `noarch_platforms` escape-hatch caveat + "why local gates miss CI failures".** From opik #33936 (noarch, `if: not (linux and aarch64)` run selector + `conda-forge.yml` `noarch_platforms`): the GHA `linter` passed but the **`conda-forge-linter` webservice STILL flagged the noarch selector** — `validate_recipe` had flagged it locally and it was *wrongly dismissed* as the G12 false-positive. Lessons: the `noarch_platforms` escape hatch is **not dependable for the conda-forge-linter webservice** (worked for xorq's `if: linux`, not opik's `if: not (...)`) — never treat `validate_recipe`'s "noarch can't have selectors" as a guaranteed false-positive; and **prefer eliminating the selector via G35** — most such selectors track the upstream musllinux_aarch64 *wheel* gap, not conda availability, so if conda-forge ships the dep on all subdirs (verify per-subdir repodata; mind `_`-vs-`-`, G10) make it **unconditional** + delete the `conda-forge.yml` → green on both linters, installable everywhere. Also answers "why didn't local lint/build catch this": (1) `validate_recipe` DID catch the lint (the miss was a judgment error overriding it); (2) local `recipe-build`/`validate` run on the **host platform only**, so per-platform issues (opik's osx-64 `litellm→fastuuid` py3.10 gap, G40/G61) can't surface locally — run the G40 per-subdir repodata check for compiled transitive deps before submitting. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G12 refinement + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.46.1 → 8.46.2); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.46.1** (Jun 26, 2026) — **G64 refinement (PATCH).** The ready-for-review ping gains a third precondition: the PR must **not be a draft** (drafts aren't ready for review — pinging them is premature). G64 now pings only when **ALL** of: every check green, `isDraft == false`, and `review-requested` absent — `gh pr view <pr> --repo conda-forge/staged-recipes --json isDraft,labels`. Pre-PR Submission checklist item updated accordingly. **Files**: `SKILL.md` (G64 + checklist + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.46.0 → 8.46.1); `CHANGELOG.md`.

**v8.46.0** (Jun 26, 2026) — **review-request retro (MINOR — 1 new gotcha + G62 reinforcement).** From the qianfan #33935 review-request step: **G64** — after CI is **all-green**, request review with **one** language-matched ping (`@conda-forge/help-python` for pure-Python noarch; `help-c-cpp` / `help-rust` / `help-go` / … per language). **Check the PR's labels first**: the ping triggers a bot to add `review-requested` + the language label (e.g. `python`), so if those labels are already present a prior ping already landed → **skip** (labels are the authoritative dedup signal, not comment text). The ping is terse — exactly `@conda-forge/help-<lang>, ready for review!`. qianfan #33935 got pinged twice (manual + automated-without-checking); the duplicate was deleted. **G62 reinforcement** — the strip is **local-retains / strip-on-push**: the `cfe-*` block lives in the LOCAL `recipes/<name>/recipe.yaml` permanently (caches identity + decisions + on-cf status + build record for tooling) and is removed **only on the pushed copy**. **Never delete `cfe-*` from the local recipe** — on submission, update the local `cfe-on-conda-forge-status` → `pending-approval-on-conda-forge` and add `cfe-submission-pr:`, don't remove the block (qianfan's local cfe-removal on 2026-06-26 was an error, restored). Added a post-green review-request item to the Pre-PR Submission checklist. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G64 + G62 reinforcement + checklist item + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.45.0 → 8.46.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry).

**v8.45.0** (Jun 26, 2026) — **submission-mechanics retro (MINOR — 2 new gotchas).** From the qianfan #33935 test submission: **G62** — NEVER ship `cfe-*` metadata. The strip (remove the `extra.cfe-*` keys + `#### CFE metadata`/`# CFE comments` blocks before pushing) is a **manual, silent-if-skipped** step: rattler-build + conda-smithy ignore unknown `extra:` keys, so a recipe with cfe-metadata still builds and lints clean — only a human reviewer would catch it. So **verify it on the PUSHED artifact**, never assume: `gh api …contents/recipes/<name>/recipe.yaml?ref=<branch> | base64 -d | grep -nE 'cfe-|# CFE'` (abort if any hit) before opening the PR. This is the under-strip complement of G60 (over-strip → dropped `context:`): strip exactly the cfe block, no less (G62), no more (G60); applies to staged-recipes AND feedstock pushes. **G63** — open staged-recipes PRs with the conda-forge **template + completed checklist**: `gh pr create --body`/`--body-file` (or a custom API body) **replaces** `.github/pull_request_template.md` rather than merging, silently dropping the reviewer Checklist the `review-requested` flow relies on. Fetch the live template (lowercase path) + tick the boxes (all but the knowledge-base line; the maintainer-confirmation box is self-satisfied when the sole maintainer is the submitter). Both added as Pre-PR Quality-Gate Submission checklist gates. A full audit of all open + merged langflow-closure PRs confirmed **zero** cfe-metadata leaks (the strip had held — but it had been unverified). **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G62/G63 + 2 checklist gates + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.44.0 → 8.45.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry).

**v8.44.0** (Jun 26, 2026) — **PR-debugging + sed→patch-sweep retro (MINOR — 3 new gotchas + 1 refinement).** A session that debugged 4 langflow-closure staged-recipes PRs to green and ran a repo-wide in-build-`sed`→source-patch conversion surfaced: **G59** — prefer a **SOURCE PATCH** over an in-build `sed` for editing upstream source. Bare `sed -i 'script' file` (no backup-suffix) fails on macOS/**BSD sed** (`extra characters at the end of p command`), and `noarch:python` recipes build on linux **and osx and win**, so any in-build sed runs on osx; reviewers (ocefpaf, #33895) also prefer patches as more auditable/maintainable. Move the edit to `source.patches:` (top-level for multi-output → applies once to the shared source); generate by applying the exact edit to the real pinned source + `diff -u` with `a/`,`b/` prefixes. Exception: an edit that interpolates `${{ version }}` can't be a static patch → use portable `sed -i.bak … && rm -f *.bak`. Verify via the built wheel METADATA (`Requires-Dist:`, distinguishing main vs `; extra ==`-marked) + `noarch/`-vs-`broken/` placement (graph-retriever #33913, pksuid #33895; repo-wide sweep). **G60** — the strip-before-push must remove ONLY `extra.cfe-*` keys + the two `# CFE …` blocks, **never** the schema header or `context:`; dropping `context:` makes `${{ version }}` undefined → `Jinja template error … undefined value` render-fail on **every** platform (langchain-litellm #33917). **G61** — GitHub `archive/<commit>.tar.gz` sha256 **drifts** when GitHub re-gzips → source-fetch `sha256 checksum validation failed` before the build; recompute (`curl -sL <url> | sha256sum`) and prefer release/sdist tarballs; a latent risk for all commit-pinned GitHub-archive recipes (suite-st-transfers). **G40 refinement** — per-platform variant: a noarch consumer's real `python_min` can be forced by a **compiled** transitive dep that ships a Python version on some conda subdirs but not others — `fastuuid 0.14.0` has py3.10 on linux-64/win-64 but only py3.11+ on **osx-64**, so langchain-litellm #33917 (via litellm) is genuinely py3.11+; diagnose via per-subdir repodata. The sed→patch sweep (graph-retriever, pksuid, gibr, dataprofiler, agent-lifecycle-toolkit, db-gpt, milvus-lite, opendsstar, jigsawstack, langflow-base/langflow/langflow-suite, suite-*) all rebuilt+tested GREEN; repo now has **zero bare `sed -i`**. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G59/G60/G61 + G40 refinement + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.43.0 → 8.44.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry).

**v8.43.0** (Jun 25, 2026) — **langflow-closure submission-session retro (MINOR — 3 new gotchas + 2 refinements).** A long multi-PR staged-recipes session (ibm-cos-suite + ~19 langflow-closure PRs + an impit platform-expansion) surfaced: **G56** — multi-output `noarch:python` build scripts run on win-64 too, so a bash `cd "$SRC_DIR/<sub>"` + `"$PYTHON"` per-output script fails on cmd.exe; use `${{ PYTHON }} -m pip install ./<sub>` (jinja interpreter + relative subdir path). The repo's `crewai-suite` carries the same latent bug (ibm-cos-suite #33886, buildId 1543755). **G57** — a build-control env var set only via bash `export` (e.g. `PYCBC_OPENSSL_DIR`) is UNSET on win-64, so the build silently falls back to a network fetch (CMake FetchContent OpenSSL → 404); set it cross-platform after reading the upstream build code to confirm the var steers the build (couchbase #33893, buildId 1543796). **G58** — run `lookup_feedstock` BEFORE every staged-recipes submission: a package already on conda-forge is rejected by the GHA `linter.py` "Feedstock with the same name exists" check even while the linting-*service* bot says "excellent" (trust the GHA linter); load-bearing for dep-closure efforts (impit #33897 → closed, repurposed as a platform-expansion mirror). **G19 refinement** — not Rust-specific: any win-64 build reading a non-ASCII file with the default cp1252 codec (pure-setuptools `setup.py open('README.md')` on a UTF-8 README) → `UnicodeDecodeError: charmap`; same `PYTHONUTF8: "1"` fix (lomond #33889). **G26 refinement** — poetry-core builds the wheel METADATA from the sdist's bundled `PKG-INFO`, NOT `pyproject.toml`, so a pyproject-only loosen sed passes LOCALLY but fails staged-recipes CI; patch all three (`pyproject.toml`+`PKG-INFO`+`setup.py`) (pksuid #33895). **Workflow**: an adversarial BFS **closure audit** (cross-check every `run`+`run_constraints` dep against `cf ∪ local-recipes`) proves a dep-closure spec has ZERO unpackaged gaps + surfaces authored-but-unlisted prereqs — a closure spec MUST name every blocker + list every net-new prereq (the langflow spec was missing 9). **impit platform-expansion**: Rust cross-compile to linux-aarch64 verified GREEN locally; canonical compiled-Rust expansion `conda-forge.yml` = `build_platform: {linux_aarch64: linux_64}` + `provider: {osx_arm64, linux_aarch64}` + `test: native_and_emulated`.

**v8.42.2** (Jun 24, 2026) — **wheel→source sweep retro (PATCH).** A `grep -rl 'cfe-source-kind:\s*pypi-wheel' recipes/` sweep refined the v8.42.0 source-preference rules (no new gotcha). **G54**: added a retroactive-sweep note (recipes generated before v8.42.0 may sit on a wheel when source exists — audit + re-decide) and **corrected the case study** — the `ibm-watsonx-orchestrate-{core,clients}` "keep the wheel" decision was overturned: their sdists are metadata-only, but the ADK monorepo ships source at `packages/{core,clients}` → migrated to GitHub source, GREEN (*empty sdist ≠ no source*); plus a monorepo-subdir wrinkle (build from the FULL extraction — a subdir's dynamic version may read `../../src/<pkg>/__init__.py`, so isolating it → G39 `0.0.0`). **G55**: the `setup_requires` / build-time network-fetch trap — a source build runs `setup.py`'s legacy `setup_requires` (or any net fetch) that a LOCAL build masks but conda-forge's OFFLINE CI fails on; strip it (`jigsawstack` `pytest-runner`) or host it (*a clean local source build ≠ proof of offline-CI build*). **cfe-source-kind**: keep it synced with `source:` — a stale `pypi-wheel` (live: `pybase62`, already a GitHub tag) mis-routes regens + hides the recipe from the sweep. Sweep migrations: `jigsawstack`, `ibm-watsonx-orchestrate-{core,clients}`, `lfx`; `pybase62` metadata-fixed.

**v8.42.1** (Jun 23, 2026) — **langflow-closure retro — convention clarification (PATCH).** No new gotcha; verified v8.42.0's G54/G55 source-preference + build-backend rules held across the closure. (1) Clarified the `extra.cfe-*` convention: recording the **first** local build on a recipe that has **no** `cfe-*` block (common for older pre-convention recipes — `firecrawl-py`, `mem0ai` carried only `recipe-maintainers`) means adding the **full** canonical block, not a `cfe-local-build-*`-only six-field stub — the failure mode caught in local-recipes PR #24's first draft. (2) Re-grounded `docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md` to current repo state (PRs #23–#27 merged → spec's "PR #25 (open)" + "only firecrawl-py lacks a build record" corrected; skill ref v8.35.0/G43 → v8.42.0/G55). The session's other findings were **staged-recipes-fork CI** mechanics — project-level, landed in auto-memory not the skill: the staged-recipes linter's hard-coded `{owner}/staged-recipes` repo-target 404s on a fork (use `github.repository`); the **ungated** `environment.yaml`↔`pixi.toml` sync check reds every PR until resynced (`pixi project export conda-environment -e build`); and the `maintenance` label suppresses the linter's "outside `recipes/`" lint for non-recipe (docs/CI) PRs. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (cfe-block first-build clarification + version-history entry); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.42.0 → 8.42.1); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry).

**v8.42.0** (Jun 23, 2026) — **Two new source-selection gotchas (G54 `sdist > github-source > wheel` + usable-source verify; G55 build-backend-in-host for source builds).** **MINOR bump** — additive: 2 Recipe-Authoring-Gotchas + a wheel-note enhancement; no code/test/CLI/build change. From the **langflow closure** (`docs/specs/langflow-conda-forge.md`): ~13 recipes had been emitted sourcing PyPI **wheels** (grayskull / `recipe-generator.py`'s fallback when no PyPI sdist) **without ever checking GitHub for source**, and a wheel→sdist switch then hit *"No valid build backend found … using pip."* **G54** — source preference is `usable-sdist > GitHub-source > wheel`; the generator never checked GitHub for wheel-only PyPI packages, and a naive sdist switch ships `ModuleNotFoundError`/`0.0.0`. Decision order with a usable-source check (`curl -sL <sdist> | tar -tzf - | grep -c '\.py$'` > 0 — many sdists are metadata-only/broken: `ibm-watsonx-orchestrate-*` 0 `.py`, `jigsawstack` omits a `requirements.txt` its build reads); else the GitHub tag archive (monorepo subdir via a `monorepo_tag` context var + `pip install ./src/<sub>`; autotick can't dual-bump version≠tag); wheel only as a documented last resort, with a post-switch re-verify (G7 import name, G39 version≠`0.0.0`, pip_check). **G55** — a source build runs PEP 517 → needs the `[build-system]` backend in `host` (wheel installs don't, so wheel recipes carry only `host:[python,pip]`; a wheel→source switch surfaces it). Backend map setuptools / hatchling / flit-core / poetry-core / pdm-backend / scikit-build-core / maturin / `uv-build` (G10 hyphen). **Applied live**: `langflow-sdk` wheel→GitHub-monorepo source (`src/sdk`, hatchling) GREEN; `ibm-watsonx-orchestrate-{core,clients}` reverted to wheel (metadata-only sdists, 0 `.py`). **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G54, G55 + critical-constraint wheel note); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.41.0 → 8.42.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.42.0.

**v8.41.0** (Jun 21, 2026) — **Two new bulk-sweep gotchas (G52 local-channel pollution, G53 maintainer-list re-merge).** **MINOR bump** — additive: 2 Recipe-Authoring-Gotchas sections; no code/test/CLI/build change. From the **co-maintainer total-coverage sweep** (`docs/specs/co-maintainer-feedstock-refresh.md` — the 232 co-maintained half + the sole-spec Wave H total-coverage follow-up; goal = all 769 feedstocks rxm7706 can modify in build-green `recipe.yaml`) — pilot + first scaled batch (8 recipes, all GREEN, uncommitted for review). **G52** — a multi-recipe sweep building into ONE shared `--output-dir` poisons that local channel: a locally-built NEWER version (`fixedint 0.2.0`) shadows the OLDER conda-forge version (`fixedint 0.1.6`) a *different* recipe's transitive deps need under strict channel priority → a FALSE `build-clean-test-blocked`; fix = isolated per-recipe `--output-dir build_artifacts/<sweep>/<recipe>`; suspect pollution before recording a test-block. Case: `azure-monitor-opentelemetry`. **G53** — refreshing an existing multi-maintainer feedstock must RE-MERGE the deployed `extra.recipe-maintainers` (grayskull/`generate_recipe_from_pypi` emits only the invoker → silently drops co-maintainers, incl. team handles `conda-forge/<team>`); ensure local set ⊇ deployed set before leaving any refreshed recipe. Cases: `airflow-code-editor` (dropped `xylar`), `alang` (dropped `praeclarum`) — both caught + restored by the rule. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G52, G53); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.40.0 → 8.41.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.41.0.

**v8.40.0** (Jun 21, 2026) — **Six new feedstock-refresh build-shape gotchas (G46–G51) + three feedstock-refresh refinements (source-kind verify, gh-numbering method, behind-list misclassification).** **MINOR bump** — additive: 6 new Recipe-Authoring-Gotchas sections + 3 refinements to the feedstock-platform-expansion guide; no code/test/CLI/build change. From the bulk **sole-maintainer feedstock refresh** (Waves C/D/E, ~197 recipes refreshed to feedstock-current; C1 = feedstock-still-v0 keep-meta+author-v1, C2 = feedstock-v1 rm-meta; all uncommitted for review). **New gotchas**: (1) **G46** — a stale local `meta.yaml`'s `noarch: python` flag can be WRONG for a genuinely-compiled package; the CURRENT sdist is the source of truth (the "local-meta-is-wrong" sibling of G42 — G42 distrusts *reputation*, G46 distrusts the *stale local meta*). Case: `hll` (C extension, import `HLL`) + `skranger` (Cython/C++ over ranger) were stale-noarch; corrected to compiled. (2) **G47** — a stale git-tracked recipe-dir `conda_build_config.yaml` that's a verbatim copy of the global pinning CBC (zero recipe-specific keys) breaks the build two ways: conda-smithy lint baseline errors (MACOSX_DEPLOYMENT_TARGET / c_stdlib_version below baseline) AND a hard variant `duplicate entry "<key>"` collision (rattler-build auto-discovers a recipe-adjacent CBC). Sanctioned fix: `mv …bak` for the build, restore for review, flag the tracked file for deletion (deployed feedstocks have none). Case: `hll` + `jh2` (`duplicate entry "libitk_devel"`). (3) **G48** — "Rust/Go upstream" ≠ heavy from-source compile; verify the actual PEP-517 backend before sizing the build or adding `compiler('cxx')`. Case: `wasmtime-py`'s sdist has NO `Cargo.toml`/`.rs` — its backend downloads a precompiled wasmtime C-API binary at build (~46 s); a speculative `cxx` was correctly dropped. (4) **G49** — per-Python compiled ≠ abi3; verify `py_limited_api`/`pyo3/abi3-*` in `Cargo.toml`/`setup.py` before adding `version_independent`+`python-abi3`; a per-Python artifact needs a SIMPLE imports+pip_check test, NOT the CFEP-25 cross-version triad (build-shape sibling of G38). Case: `json-stream-rs-tokenizer` wrongly carried `version_independent`+`python-abi3`+`OPENSSL_DIR` hack but its Cargo PyO3 features carry no abi3 → per-Python; dropped all three, mirrored the feedstock, simple test. (5) **G50** — a newer CPython that drops a private C-API symbol (or a host pin with no new-cpython wheel) breaks a compiled build / host solve; cap the matrix with `build.skip: match(python, ">=N")` (v1 form, NOT `py<N` which G3 says is silently ignored), mirroring upstream's published range. Cases: `psycopg2-yugabytedb` (py3.13 removed `_PyInterpreterState_Get`) + `datasketches` (host `numpy<2.0`, no numpy-1.x cp313 wheel) → both `skip: match(python, ">=3.13")`. (6) **G51** — a GitHub monorepo subdir may ship NONE of the release-time-generated assets (web `www/`, codegen) that exist only in the published PyPI wheel; a from-source GitHub build yields a broken empty package — and the DEPLOYED feedstock may already ship that broken package (flag as a REAL BUG). Inverse of G5 (there the GitHub source is complete and the sdist is stripped; here the wheel is complete and the GitHub source is incomplete). Fix: source the PyPI wheel. Case: `h2o-lightwave-web` — GitHub subdir ships zero `www/` assets; from-source build → broken empty ~15 KiB package; deployed feedstock likely ships it; sourced the wheel (1.8.9 is wheel-only). **Refinements** (to `guides/feedstock-platform-expansion.md` Wave A): (7) **source-kind verify is a strong default** — across the whole `wagtail-*`/`django-*`/`h2o-*`/`kedro`/`copilotkit`/`pypac`/`acachecontrol`/`collectfasta`/`spec-kit` batch the deployed feedstocks source from a GitHub-tag archive, not the PyPI sdist; read the deployed `source.url` and mirror its kind, set the cached `cfe-source-kind` to the verified value. (8) **gh-numbering method** — a "behind" numbering flag is usually a REAL behind with aligned numbering (`v`-prefix only); a true false-positive is rare and almost always an npm-monorepo (monorepo GH tag ≠ sub-package PyPI version). Distinguish via deployed feedstock version+source → PyPI vs GitHub histories → for a monorepo, the sub-package's `pyproject` `version` at the tag + sha256 identity. Of 13 numbering-risk recipes (Jun 2026), only **copilotkit** was a true false-positive (GH `v1.57.2` == PyPI `copilotkit` 0.1.88, same code); the other 12 were genuinely behind. (9) **behind-list misclassification** — a baseline list can flag a LOCAL-ONLY recipe as on-cf; always `lookup_feedstock` to confirm existence before any C2 (rm-meta.yaml) transition — `exists:false` → keep meta.yaml, set `pending-submission-to-conda-forge`; also watch two-feedstock collisions. Cases: **cookiecutter-django** (no feedstock; PyPI abandoned at 1.11.9; GitHub CalVer tag) → kept local-only; **spec-kit** (`spec-kit-feedstock` github-tag vs competing `specify-cli-feedstock` pypi-sdist). **Reconfirmations** (existing guidance held; no new gotcha): kedro 1.x py3.14 warning-as-error → test pinned to `python_min.*` (kedro-datasets Wave C + kedro-boot Wave E); **G34** setuptools<81 for pkg_resources still recurs (tabcmd 2.0.18); Django/Wagtail apps with empty `__init__.py` do NOT trip the import gotcha (standard CFEP-25 `python.imports` holds, no escape hatch — confirmed across ~20 wagtail/django recipes); license-vs-upstream-metadata mismatches (wagtailmath BSD-not-MIT, wagtailstreamforms MIT-not-Proprietary) — v1 carries the LICENSE-file-correct license, mirror stays faithful to deployed. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G46–G51); `guides/feedstock-platform-expansion.md` (Wave A source-kind + gh-numbering + behind-list refinements + G46–G51 cross-ref); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.39.0 → 8.40.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.40.0.

**v8.39.0** (Jun 20, 2026) — **New gotcha G45: a browser SPA (Vue/React/Svelte + Vite) is usually NOT conda-forge-submittable — run the viability gate first, then build local-only as a static-site + launcher.** **MINOR bump** — additive: 1 new Recipe-Authoring-Gotchas section; no code/test/CLI/build change. Sibling to G44 (the "non-standard-distribution → judgment call + local-only fallback" pair). A front-end SPA frequently fails several conda-forge bars at once, all upstream facts you can't fix: `package.json "private": true` (forbids npm publication), not on the npm registry / no PyPI dist (canonical `npm pack` pattern has nothing to pull), no GitHub releases/tags (only a moving `main`), and no `bin` (a browser app served by a web server, not a command — the right distribution is the hosted site / Docker). G45 ships a **copy-paste viability gate** (read `package.json` name/private/bin → check npm registry → check GitHub releases+tags) to run BEFORE writing any recipe, and a **local-only build pattern** for when the user opts in anyway: `noarch:generic` + `nodejs >=20` build dep; build.sh does `export BASE_URL=./` (relative asset paths) + `npm ci` + **`npx vite build`** (skip the dev-only `vue-tsc`/`tsc` type-check — doesn't change `dist/`, can break on a main-HEAD checkout); copy `dist/.` to `$PREFIX/share/<name>/` + a `$PREFIX/bin/<name>` launcher that serves it via `python -m http.server` (python run dep); GitHub-archive source pinned to a `main` commit (`cfe-source-kind: github-commit`, bump version+commit together — no autotick); `license_file: LICENSE` from the archive; tests assert index.html + launcher present; `cfe-noarch: generic`, `cfe-on-conda-forge-status: blocked-pending-prerequisites` with the upstream blockers recorded. Caveats: `npm ci` is NETWORK (fine local-only, forbidden on cf CI — another reason it's not submittable); unix bash launcher → Windows not covered; verify the built index.html uses relative `./assets/` refs (proves `BASE_URL=./` took). Explicitly distinguished from **G6** (a *published* npm CLI with a real `bin` → canonical `npm pack`, IS submittable). **Case study**: cyclonedx-bom-studio 0.9.2 (`CycloneDX/cyclonedx-bom-studio`, Apache-2.0 Vue 3 + Vite SBOM editor) — private, not-on-npm, no releases/tags, no bin → not submittable; built local-only (pinned to main commit `f2a6d30b`, `npm ci` + `npx vite build`, BASE_URL=./) into a noarch:generic package shipping the 56-file static site + a `cyclonedx-bom-studio` launcher; GREEN on linux-64; index.html verified using relative `./assets/`. Same session also mirrored + locally built the two *submittable* siblings already on conda-forge (`cyclonedx-python-lib` multi-output + `cyclonedx-bom`) — the contrast is the lesson: Python lib/CLI belong on conda-forge, the browser SPA does not. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G45); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.38.0 → 8.39.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.39.0.

**v8.38.0** (Jun 20, 2026) — **New gotcha G44: .NET / C# CLI tools have NO source-build path on conda-forge — repackage the self-contained release binaries per-platform.** **MINOR bump** — additive: 1 new Recipe-Authoring-Gotchas section + `github-release-binary` added to the `cfe-source-kind` enum (the example at line 213 + the value-semantics explanation); no code/test/CLI/build change. **First .NET tool packaged in this repo** (cyclonedx-cli 0.32.0, this session). conda-forge has **no `dotnet-sdk` and no `dotnet-runtime` feedstock** (verified 2026-06-20 — both `lookup_feedstock` return `exists=False`), and the hermetic build sandbox forbids `dotnet restore`'s NuGet network fetch, so a from-source .NET build is a **dead end** — fundamentally unlike Rust/Go, which have conda-forge toolchains + a vendored-dependency story. G44 documents the **binary-repackage** pattern: per-platform single-file `source:` entries gated by target-platform selectors (each with `file_name:` + sha256, no archive extraction), build script copies to `bin/` (unix, +x) / `Library\bin` (win), **no `compiler()`/`stdlib()`** (nothing is compiled → STD-001 N/A), **no run-deps** (the .NET self-contained binary bundles the runtime), **NOT noarch** (each artifact is a per-platform binary → `cfe-noarch: compiled`), **ship LICENSE in-recipe** (the bare binaries carry none — canonical License-File pattern (2)), test `<tool> --version`. Caveats captured: binary-repackaging draws conda-forge reviewer scrutiny (decide submit-vs-local-only up front per the Ask-First boundary; record in `cfe-on-conda-forge-status` + `cfe-forge-blocker-list`); upstream ships more arches than conda-forge has subdirs for (musl / linux-arm armv7 / win-x86 / win-arm64 have no cf subdir → standard-5 only, state the drops); .NET globalization may need `icu` and TLS may need `openssl` at runtime in a clean conda env (`Couldn't find a valid ICU package` → add to `run:` or set `DOTNET_SYSTEM_GLOBALIZATION_INVARIANT=1`); no upstream checksums file is typical → compute each sha256 by streaming (`curl -sSL <url> | sha256sum`), don't download-then-hash 5 × ~80 MB. **New `cfe-source-kind: github-release-binary`** value for repackaged prebuilt single-file binaries. **Case study**: cyclonedx-cli 0.32.0 (`CycloneDX/cyclonedx-cli`, Apache-2.0 .NET 8 SBOM CLI) — repackaged the 5 self-contained release binaries (linux-x64/arm64, osx-x64/arm64, win-x64) with **zero run-deps**; dropped the musl / linux-arm / win-x86 / win-arm64 assets; linux-64 leg built GREEN and the packaged binary ran `cyclonedx --version` → `0.32.0` (exit 0), the other 4 legs sha256-verified but not executed locally (cross-platform on a linux-64 host); kept **local-only** (`cfe-on-conda-forge-status: pending-submission-to-conda-forge`) pending the binary-repackage submission decision. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G44 + `cfe-source-kind` enum in 2 places); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.37.0 → 8.38.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.38.0.

**v8.37.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **Tier-1 cfe-* identity/decision fields (4 new) + retire 3 dead SBOM placeholders + a schema design-principle note.** **MINOR bump** — additive local-recipes-only `extra.cfe-*` schema + 1 design-principle subsection; no code/test/CLI/build change. From the **4-analyst deep-analysis synthesis** (2026-06-19) of which `cfe-*` fields actually earn their place. **4 new fields** placed in the `# CFE metadata` block immediately after `cfe-upstream-homepage` (end of the identity/upstream block, before `cfe-on-conda-forge-status`): (1) **`cfe-import-names: [...]`** — the **verified** top-level Python import name(s) (the CFEP-25 test `imports:`); caches the G7/G10 distribution-vs-import divergence (`altk`, `OpenDsStar`, `pymilvus.model`, `ibm_boto3`, `baidubce`, `data_diff`) so a regen RESTORES the correct value instead of letting grayskull re-guess it wrong off the sdist — the single highest-frequency authoring recompute, especially load-bearing for the feedstock-refresh effort (256 regens); non-Python recipes carry `[]`. (2) **`cfe-source-kind`** — `pypi-sdist | pypi-wheel | github-tag | github-commit`; append `:<reason>` when a non-PyPI source was deliberately chosen (e.g. `github-tag:pypi-sdist-strips-headers-G5`) so a version bump can't silently revert to a sdist that re-trips G4/G5/G9/G16. (3) **`cfe-noarch`** — `python | generic | compiled`; drives the build matrix + per-Python prereq fan-out (G38/G40); per G42 it can flip across versions (milvus-lite 3.0 C++→pure-python). (4) **`cfe-pip-check`** — `true | false:<reason-code>`; when off, the `false:<reason-code>` records the temporary external-bug waiver + its revert obligation (G24/G26/G28/G36) so it isn't silently lost on strip-before-push. **New "cfe-* schema design principle" subsection** (3 rules): (a) CACHE identity + hard-won decisions, READ volatile metrics live from the atlas (CVE/downloads/feedstock-health/adoption-stage/who-depends are NEVER cached — caching manufactures staleness); (b) STAMP any cacheable-but-volatile field with `cfe-last-checked` as a hint, never ground truth; (c) all `cfe-*` are stripped before any push. **Placeholder retirement**: the deep-analysis disqualified the three previously-floated SBOM/security placeholders — **`cfe-cpe`** (CPE is syft-derived from package name → recompute), **`cfe-sbom-hash`** (SBOM's home is `conda-meta/` per unratified CEP #127), **`cfe-syft-ref`** (attestation lives in an external Sigstore bundle); none reaches a tool from recipe `extra:`. (None of the three was ever encoded in any skill file — verified by grep across `SKILL.md` + `reference/` + `guides/` + `quickref/`; the note records the disqualification so they're never re-floated.) **Tier-2-PLANNED note**: `cfe-feedstock-version` + `cfe-upstream-latest-version` (the cached legs of the behind-upstream triple, stamped-hint), `cfe-platforms-shipping` / `cfe-platforms-target` (platform coverage), and `cfe-submission-pr-state` (completes `cfe-submission-pr`) land WITH the feedstock-refresh effort, where they get populated. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (4 fields in the cfe-* metadata example + identity/decision value-semantics block + the design-principle subsection w/ placeholder-retirement + Tier-2 note, all under the "Never Add AI Comments Inline" Critical Constraint); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.36.0 → 8.37.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.37.0.

**v8.36.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **New cfe-* schema rows: the LOCAL-BUILD verification record (`cfe-local-build-status` + 3 companions).** **MINOR bump** — additive local-recipes-only `extra.cfe-*` schema; no code/test/CLI/build change. Separates **"does it build locally"** (a verified fact) from **"is it on conda-forge"** (`cfe-on-conda-forge-status`): a `blocked-pending-prerequisites` recipe may have built **perfectly** locally (green against the local channel) and is "blocked" only because a prereq isn't on conda-forge yet — the new field records that the recipe itself is sound. **4 new rows** (placed in the `# CFE metadata` block immediately after `cfe-generated-at-datetime`): **`cfe-local-build-status`** (`success` = build EXIT=0 AND import test AND pip_check all pass, artifact in `noarch/`/`linux-64/`; **`build-clean-test-blocked`** = build phase clean / `.conda` written but the test-env solve failed on a missing/local-only/not-yet-on-cf dep, rattler quarantines to `broken/` — recipe is sound, the block is a prerequisite gap, the common langflow-closure case; `failed` = build phase itself failed; `not-attempted` = authored-not-built, the **default** the recipe-generator emits), **`cfe-local-build-datetime`** (ISO-8601 UTC | `none`), **`cfe-local-build-platform`** (host subdir the build ran on, e.g. `linux-64` | `none`), **`cfe-local-build-tool`** (`rattler-build` v1 / `conda-build` v0 | `none`). Always set from the ACTUAL last-build outcome, never inferred from cf-submission status. All four are stripped before any push like every `cfe-*` key. **`recipe-generator.py` does NOT emit the cfe-* block** (verified — only `cfe-sdist-cache` temp dir matches), so no generator change; the `not-attempted` default is documented for when generator-emission is wired (still flagged pending since v8.31.0). No reference/*.md file enumerates the cfe-* schema (it lives only in SKILL.md), so only SKILL.md was edited. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (4 fields in the cfe-* metadata example + value-semantics block under the "Never Add AI Comments Inline" Critical Constraint); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.35.0 → 8.36.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). **v8.35.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **langflow full-prereq-closure retro: 5 new gotchas (G39–G43) + an external-cf-skew Build-Failure-Protocol note.** **MINOR bump** — additive: 5 gotchas + 1 BFP subsection; no code/test/schema/CLI change. From this session's ~25-recipe authoring wave across 4 recursion layers to make langflow locally buildable (langflow reached build-GREEN; its test-env solve is blocked by irreducible external cf ecosystem version-skew). **G39** — setuptools_scm private-API `_version_helper`: an sdist wiring its version via `[tool.setuptools.dynamic] version = {attr = ...}` pointing at a `_version_helper.py`/`_version.py` that imports PRIVATE setuptools_scm internals (`_types`, `Configuration`, `fallbacks`, `version.*`) removed in setuptools_scm 8.x fails cf metadata generation with `ImportError: cannot import name '_types'`; fix by shipping a checked-in idempotent `pin_version.py` that rewrites `pyproject.toml` to a static `$PKG_VERSION` + strips the dynamic-version machinery as the FIRST build step, then drop `setuptools-scm`/`gitpython` from host. Case: pymilvus-model 0.3.2. **G40** (refines G38) — version-level Python-floor drop: a dep can DROP a Python version in a newer release (ibm-watsonx-ai 1.5.x needs py>=3.11; 1.3.37 was the last py3.10 line), so a noarch consumer with python_min 3.10 can't resolve the dep's latest build on its py3.10 test leg; either ALSO build the dep's last py3.10 version into the channel OR raise the consumer's python_min; always collapse the dep's per-Python markers to the broadest floor (G35). Case: ibm-watsonx-ai / langchain-ibm / langflow. **G41** — hidden py3.11 floor via unconditional PEP-655 / new-stdlib import: a hard dep that unconditionally imports a version-gated stdlib symbol with NO fallback (jsonquerylang imports `typing.NotRequired`, PEP 655 = py3.11+, in EVERY version) forces the consumer's REAL python_min to that floor regardless of the consumer's declared `requires-python >=3.10`; set python_min to the MAX of all transitive hard Python floors, don't trust the upstream lower bound alone. Case: langflow/langflow-base → jsonquerylang. **G42** — verify the CURRENT version's artifact shape before assuming compiled: build shape can change across versions (milvus-lite was a C++ binary-wheel through 2.4/2.5 but 3.0 is a pure-Python rewrite — faiss-cpu/pyarrow backend, `py3-none-any` wheel, `Root-Is-Purelib: true`, zero `.so`); always inspect the LATEST sdist/wheel (`.so/.pyd` presence, `Root-Is-Purelib`) rather than inferring from an older version's reputation; the pure-Python path is simpler AND cf-submittable. Case: milvus-lite 3.0. **G43** — v1 inline-comment-on-list-items trips conda-smithy comment-selector lint: a trailing `# comment` on a YAML list item (even inside `extra:`) is parsed by conda-smithy as a potential selector and flagged; use FULL-LINE comments ABOVE the item, reinforcing the comments-at-bottom convention (v8.31.0). Case: langflow recipe cfe-* block. **External-cf-skew BFP note** — Build Failure Protocol subsection "External conda-forge ecosystem version-skew (not a recipe defect)": when a full-dependency-graph test-env solve fails but each conflicting sub-cluster solves IN ISOLATION on conda-forge, the cause is cross-feedstock pin skew (cf `litellm` baking `fastapi==0.124.4` vs a consumer needing `fastapi>=0.135`; an otel/`traceloop-sdk`/`openinference-*`/`langchain` observability cluster with mutually-incompatible pins), NOT a recipe defect; do NOT churn the consumer — document the conflicting packages + pins in `cfe-forge-blocker-list`, set `cfe-on-conda-forge-status: blocked-pending-prerequisites`, and STOP (resolution requires upstream feedstock pin convergence). Case: langflow → lfx/litellm/traceloop. **Convention verification**: the cfe-* + comments-at-bottom convention (v8.31.0–v8.34.0) was applied to ~25 new recipes across the langflow prereq-closure authoring wave with no corrections needed; G35 (per-Python marker collapse) was successfully applied to ibm-watsonx-ai, langchain-ibm, agent-lifecycle-toolkit, and langflow. One cleanup pending in a recipe (primp used the legacy status value token), tracked separately. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G39–G43 in Recipe Authoring Gotchas; external-cf-skew subsection in Build Failure Protocol); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.34.0 → 8.35.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.35.0.

**v8.34.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **langflow-prereq session retro: 4 new gotchas (G35–G38) + a non-OSI license-eligibility note.** **MINOR bump** — additive: 4 gotchas + 1 Policy bullet; no code/test/schema/CLI change. From this session's langflow-prereq builds, cfe-* convention rollout, Wave-2 straggler builds, and the langflow capstone attempt. **G35** — noarch numpy env-marker selector collapse (a G12 refinement): a per-Python `numpy` run-dep selector on a noarch:python recipe (`if: match(python, "<3.13") / then: numpy >=1.26.4 / else: numpy >=2.1.0`) is a G12 violation — the upstream markers `numpy>=1.26.4; python_version<"3.13"` / `numpy>=2.1.0; python_version>="3.13"` track numpy's OWN cp313 wheel-availability floor (numpy 2.1.0 first shipped cp313 wheels), not a per-Python package feature; collapse to the broadest floor (`numpy >=1.26.4`) and let the install-time solver pick a Python-compatible numpy. Case: langchain-google-community 5.0.0. **G36** — a stale conda-forge build whose wheel METADATA caps a dep tighter than its conda `run:` dep fails `pip check` even though the conda solve succeeds: a version can have two builds (older with a loose conda dep `mcp <2.0.0` but a tight embedded wheel cap `mcp !=1.21.1,<1.23,>=1.19.0`, and a newer metadata-patched build); the solver may pick the stale build + a too-new transitive dep, so `pip check` (reads METADATA) fails; fix by raising the OUTER package's lower bound (`fastmcp >=2.14`) to force past the stale build — a strict subset of upstream intent. Case: toolguard → fastmcp 2.13.3 stale build. **G37** — `[tool.uv]` no-build / source flags in an sdist are NOT runtime deps: a line like `apify-shared = false` under `[tool.uv]` is a uv-specific flag, not a dependency; read deps only from PEP-621 `[project.dependencies]`, never from `[tool.uv.*]` (mistaking a uv flag for a dep adds a phantom blocker and hides the real one). Case: apify-client 3.0.3 — `apify-shared = false` misread; the real blocker was `impit`. **G38** — a compiled local-only prereq built for only ONE Python blocks consumers on other Python versions: a Rust/PyO3/C-ext prereq built into the local channel for a single Python (`impit-0.13.0-py310...`) can't satisfy a consumer requiring a different/higher Python (`python >=3.11`) — unlike noarch (one artifact for all Pythons), a compiled prereq needs a build per Python in the consumer's matrix; on a test-env solve failure, check the channel artifact's `py3XX` build string against the consumer's `python_min`. Case: apify-client (py>=3.11) couldn't use the channel's py310-only impit. **License note** — Policy section: source-available / non-OSI licenses (BUSL-1.1, SSPL, Elastic-2.0, Commons-Clause) are valid SPDX identifiers but are NOT conda-forge-eligible; flag them at recipe-authoring time (in `cfe-on-conda-forge-status` reasoning + the bottom CFE comments) as a submission blocker — a clean local build does not imply cf-eligibility. Case: ragstack-ai-knowledge-store (BUSL-1.1). **Convention verification**: the cfe-* convention shipped in v8.31.0–v8.33.0 (comments-at-bottom + cfe-on-conda-forge-status schema + meta.yaml mirror rule) held across the 89-recipe session rollout and the Wave-2 straggler build verification with no corrections needed. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (G35–G38 in Recipe Authoring Gotchas; non-OSI license bullet in Policy); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.33.0 → 8.34.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.34.0.

**v8.33.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **Migration Protocol: local-mirror fidelity — keep `meta.yaml` until the feedstock itself migrates to `recipe.yaml`.** **MINOR bump** — additive guidance; no code/test/CLI/schema change. User-established. For a `recipes/<name>/` that mirrors an existing conda-forge feedstock, the local mirror MUST match the feedstock's CURRENT format: if the feedstock still ships `meta.yaml` (v0), **keep `meta.yaml`** (pull the latest from the feedstock) AND author the v1 `recipe.yaml` alongside it — both coexist (`meta.yaml` = un-annotated deployed mirror; `recipe.yaml` = our v1 with CFE metadata that captures `cfe-on-conda-forge-status: confirmed-on-conda-forge` + `cfe-forge-recipe-updates-needed: meta-yaml-to-recipe-yaml` + the blocker list). Delete `meta.yaml` ONLY after the feedstock completes its v0→v1 switch (migration PR merges), not when the local build succeeds. Pre-emptively converting a still-v0 mirror to v1 diverges it from what's deployed, so an edit copied back up wouldn't match. Bounds the existing "Migrate when actively updated" trigger: convert the mirror only when YOU drive the feedstock migration (the `cfe-forge-recipe-updates-needed: meta-yaml-to-recipe-yaml` token, v8.32.0, flags one still needing it). **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (Migration Protocol § When to Migrate); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.32.0 → 8.33.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry); auto-memory `feedback_keep_meta_yaml_until_feedstock_migrates.md` + `MEMORY.md` index. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.33.0.

**v8.32.0** (Jun 19, 2026) — **cfe-* metadata schema finalization: `cfe-status` → `cfe-on-conda-forge-status` (new token vocabulary) + 3 new forge-tracking rows.** **MINOR bump** — additive schema; local-recipes-only `extra.cfe-*` convention; no code/test/CLI/build change. User-finalized this session. (1) **Field rename** `cfe-status` → `cfe-on-conda-forge-status` with a clearer token set: `confirmed-on-conda-forge` (was on-conda-forge), `pending-approval-on-conda-forge` (submitted, in review), `pending-submission-to-conda-forge` (builds green locally, ready), `blocked-pending-prerequisites` (**new** — builds locally but a prereq isn't on cf / an upstream feedstock needs a bump; e.g. langchain-elasticsearch, pksuid→pybase62, langchain-google-vertexai→google-cloud-vectorsearch), `pypi-only`, `archived-on-conda-forge`. (2) **3 new rows**: `cfe-on-conda-forge-feedstock` (feedstock URL when confirmed/archived, else `none`), `cfe-forge-recipe-updates-needed` (default `none` for everything with nothing queued, else a list from a 14-token maintenance vocabulary — meta-yaml-to-recipe-yaml / recipe-regenerate / rerender / version-bump / add-build-platforms / python-matrix-update / add-maintainers / dependency-fix / add-run-exports / test-fix / license-fix / mark-broken / yank; `recipe-v1-to-v2` reserved for a future schema_version 2), `cfe-forge-blocker-list` (YAML list, `[]` when none — runtime blockers for confirmed pkgs, prereq blockers for blocked-pending-prerequisites). Both new sections sit inside the `#### CFE metadata AND comments` / `# CFE metadata` block (paired with v8.31.0's `# CFE comments` block); all `cfe-*` content is local-only and stripped before any push. **Test**: applied to `recipes/{ironcalc (confirmed-on-conda-forge), metaphor-python (pending-submission-to-conda-forge), podman-desktop (confirmed + Hyper-V blocker)}` — three states validated consistent. **Files touched**: `SKILL.md` (concrete cfe-* schema in the comments-constraint example); `config/skill-config.yaml` (8.31.0 → 8.32.0); `CHANGELOG.md` (this entry); auto-memory `feedback_extra_is_local_internal_metadata.md` (schema + token vocabularies). **Pending**: roll the rename + 3 rows + comment relocation across the other ~57 session recipes.
