**v8.15.0** (Jun 12, 2026) — **Phase P incremental BigQuery refresh** + schema v26 `pypi_downloads_daily` side table. **MINOR bump** — additive: new table + new env vars + new test file + new reference doc; no change to the consumer surface (`pypi_intelligence.downloads_30d/90d` columns unchanged; readers don't know the difference). Spec: `docs/specs/atlas-phase-p-incremental.md`. Driver: complete the v8.14.3 hot-patch by replacing the single-shot 90-day query with an incremental architecture that drives sustained refresh cost below $1/run while preserving full per-package exactness across the ~600k PyPI namespace. **Wave A — Schema v26 + Phase P refactor**: (1) new `pypi_downloads_daily(pypi_name TEXT, download_date TEXT, downloads INTEGER, PK(pypi_name, download_date))` table + 2 indexes; CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS handled at the SCHEMA_DDL level so existing init_schema picks it up idempotently. SCHEMA_VERSION bumped 25 → 26. (2) `phase_p_pypi_downloads` rewritten: mode-selection logic (`first-pull` when table empty; `incremental` when populated with gap ≤ 90d; `first-pull-after-gap` when gap > 90d with warning logged; `no-op` early return when no new partitions); `_PARTITIONDATE` literal-date query GROUP BY (pypi_name, _PARTITIONDATE) returning per-day per-package rows; bulk INSERT OR IGNORE into `pypi_downloads_daily` filtered to `downloads >= 1` (zero-count days implicit absence); SQL aggregation INSERT ... ON CONFLICT updates `pypi_intelligence.downloads_30d/90d` from local table; GC deletes rows older than `PHASE_P_RETAIN_DAYS` (default 95 — 5d slack beyond 90d window). All inside one BEGIN/COMMIT for atomicity. (3) New tunables: `PHASE_P_RETAIN_DAYS=95`, `PHASE_P_FORCE_FIRST_PULL=1` (wipes table for clean re-bootstrap). Deprecation warning logged if `PHASE_P_BQ_WINDOW_DAYS` is set (was declared in v8.1.0 spec but never consumed; window is now mode-determined). New `_phase_p_skip` helper DRYs the 6 early-exit paths. Return dict gains `mode`, `window_start`, `window_end`, `rows_inserted`, `rows_pruned`; `source` value changes from `'bigquery-public'` to `'bigquery-incremental'` (both remain valid in reader queries — `downloads_fetched_at` is the staleness detector). **Wave B — Tests + new reference doc**: (1) `test_phase_p_bigquery.py` gains TestPhaseP_IncrementalArchitecture class (8 cases: per-day GROUP BY shape, INSERT OR IGNORE into daily table, recompute SQL chain, GC clause, no-new-partitions short-circuit, gap-revert mode label, force-first-pull wipe, deprecated env-var warning). The existing TestPhaseP_CostGuardrails first-pull detection test updated to look for `MAX(download_date)` instead of v8.14.3's `downloads_fetched_at IS NOT NULL`. 18/18 cases pass. (2) New `test_pypi_downloads_daily.py` with 14 cases: schema migration (table exists, column types, indexes, composite PK, schema_version=26, idempotent re-init, meta-row records '26'), INSERT OR IGNORE idempotency (duplicate PK ignored vs distinct PKs both inserted), aggregation correctness (30d window excludes day-30+, 90d excludes day-95, single-day-in-window, upsert overwrites prior aggregate, GC deletes only `< cutoff`). 14/14 pass. (3) New `reference/atlas-phase-p-cost-model.md` (~430 lines) — single source of truth for cost claims: TL;DR table by mode, why-v8.1.0-was-wrong section, dry-run preflight procedure (operator-runnable via `bq query --dry_run`), hard cap behaviour (`maximum_bytes_billed` server-side aborts $0), wall-clock cap (`job_timeout_ms`), tunables reference, mode decision tree, operator runbook (routine refresh, cost-spike investigation, recovery from corruption, air-gap operator), alternative-source verification procedures (ClickHouse clickpy, ecosyste.ms, manual `bq` CLI), storage profile (~225-450 MB steady-state), annual cost projection (~$30/year v8.15.0 vs ~$200/year v8.14.3 vs ~$2,000+ pre-fix). Discipline note: cost claims in spec/code/docs MUST be paired with a dry-run preflight as the source of truth — napkin numbers without provenance are bugs. **Wave C — Closeout**: this CHANGELOG entry, skill-config bump 8.14.3 → 8.15.0, catalog annotation update. Q1/Q2/Q5/Q7 from the spec were pre-resolved (monthly cadence default, $10 default cap, 10-min job timeout, 95d retention); Q3/Q4/Q6/Q8 ship with recommendations and no implementation. **Annual cost projection**: pre-fix ~$2,000+; v8.14.3 hot-patch ~$200; v8.15.0 incremental ~$30 (first-pull $15-25 one-off; 12× refresh × ~$1 = $12). 32/32 Phase P + daily-table tests pass; 5/5 meta-test_actionable_scope tests pass (no false drift flags from the table addition). Pyright clean for new code. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.15.0.

**v8.14.3** (Jun 12, 2026) — **Phase P BigQuery cost guardrails** (hot-patch for the 2026-06-12 invoice surprise). **PATCH bump** — no schema change, no consumer-surface change; surgical refactor of one function + corrections to documented cost claims that were off by ~1000×. **Why it exists**: a recent `bootstrap-data --profile admin` run charged **$500+** against the documented "~30 GB scanned per query, within the 1 TB/month free tier" expectation. Root cause: the "~30 GB" figure was a 2016-era napkin number copied through the v8.1.0 spec, code docstring, CHANGELOG, three reference docs, and the quickref cheatsheet without re-verification. Empirical reality at the `file.project + _PARTITIONDATE` projection level is ~2.5–4 TB per run (~$15–25/run at $6.25/TB); pre-fix queries occasionally degraded to ~25–45 TB (~$170+/run) when planner pruning faltered. **Three changes in `phase_p_pypi_downloads`** (`scripts/conda_forge_atlas.py:6237`): (1) switched the partition filter from `timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 90 DAY)` to `_PARTITIONDATE >= DATE '<literal>'` with literal dates computed in Python — guarantees partition pruning regardless of planner mood; (2) added dry-run preflight via `QueryJobConfig(dry_run=True, use_query_cache=False)` that reads `total_bytes_processed` (free), prints the estimated scan size + USD cost, and aborts with a `skipped` result if the estimate exceeds the operator cap; (3) added `maximum_bytes_billed` as a hard server-side ceiling on the real query (BQ aborts and bills $0 if exceeded) plus `job_timeout_ms` (default 600 000 = 10 min) to prevent zombie jobs charging slot time. **First-pull vs. refresh detection**: queries `SELECT COUNT(*) FROM pypi_intelligence WHERE downloads_fetched_at IS NOT NULL` — empty → first-pull cap ($100 default via `PHASE_P_MAX_COST_FIRST_PULL_USD`); populated → refresh cap ($10 default via `PHASE_P_MAX_COST_USD`). Both knobs can be raised when operators want to widen the budget for one run. New tunables: `PHASE_P_MAX_COST_USD`, `PHASE_P_MAX_COST_FIRST_PULL_USD`, `PHASE_P_JOB_TIMEOUT_MS`, `PHASE_P_USD_PER_TB` (default 6.25, lets operators in non-US regions override). Return dict gains `estimated_usd`, `estimated_gb`, `cap_usd`, `mode` fields for downstream observability. **Doc corrections** across the live operator surfaces: `reference/atlas-phases-overview.md` (two sites — bullet list at L227 and § Phase P run at L299) and `quickref/commands-cheatsheet.md` L555 now show the real numbers + the dry-run preflight as the source of truth. `docs/specs/atlas-pypi-intelligence.md` (the predecessor spec where the lie originated) gains a top-of-document erratum banner pointing at this hot-patch and the v8.15.0 incremental architecture spec; the body is preserved as historical context per spec-versioning discipline. **6 new unit tests** in `test_phase_p_bigquery.py` covering: `_PARTITIONDATE` literal-date form (no `CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()`), dry-run preflight present, `maximum_bytes_billed` set, `job_timeout_ms` set, first-pull vs refresh cap distinction, and a behavioural test that mocks the bigquery module to verify dry-run-above-cap aborts the real query (`real_query_calls == []` assertion). **What this DOESN'T do**: drive sustained refresh cost below $1/run. That's the v8.15.0 incremental architecture (`docs/specs/atlas-phase-p-incremental.md`) — schema v26 `pypi_downloads_daily` side table + per-day per-package cache + recompute `downloads_30d/90d` via local SQL aggregation. The hot-patch is enough to stop the bleeding (worst case becomes a $10–100 dry-run-aborted run, not a $500 surprise); the architectural fix follows. **Annual cost projection**: pre-fix ~$170+/run × 12 runs/year ≈ $2,000+; post-hot-patch ~$15–25/run × 12 ≈ $200; post-v8.15.0 ~$1/run × 12 ≈ $12. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.14.3.

**v8.14.2** (Jun 12, 2026) — `pr_artifacts.extract_zip` layout fix: synthesize the `<platform>/` subdir from `art["platform"]` instead of parsing a non-existent inner subdir out of the Azure ZIP path. **PATCH bump** — bug fix; backward-incompatible signature only at the internal-function level (added `platform: str | None` kwarg; caller updated). **What was wrong**: v8.14.0's `extract_zip` docstring claimed Azure ships `conda-build_<job>/<platform>/*` (wrapper + inner platform subdir) and stripped one level to expose `<platform>/<file>` at dest. Real Azure shape (verified against PR #33693 buildId 1536673 with `--keep-zips`) is `conda_pkgs_<job>/<file>` — ONE level deep, no inner platform subdir. Stripping the wrapper dumps the files at the dest root; the three platform ZIPs all merged into the same flat directory next to a `repodata.json` that only knew about the last-extracted platform (osx-64 in our case). The channel was unusable via `mamba install -c file://... gh-copilot-cli` because the linux-64 and win-64 `.conda` files weren't indexed; the only path was installing the `.conda` file by absolute path. **Fix**: `extract_zip(zip_path, dest, *, platform=None, platforms=None)`. The caller (`fetch_one_build`) passes `platform=art["platform"]` — sourced from artifact metadata, the actual ground truth, not a name we hoped was inside the zip. Files land at `dest/<platform>/<file>` producing a canonical conda channel layout (`extracted/linux-64/...`, `extracted/osx-64/...`, `extracted/win-64/...`) where each subdir's `repodata.json` declares the matching `subdir` and `mamba install -c file://<extracted_dir>/ gh-copilot-cli` Just Works. The user's `--platforms` filter is now a whole-zip short-circuit (one zip = one platform; if the artifact's platform isn't in the user's allowlist, return `[]` without touching the filesystem) — cheaper and clearer than the previous per-member first-segment gate. **Security note — Zip Slip guard re-ordering**: the abs-path / `..`-traversal check now runs on the post-wrapper `inner` path BEFORE re-nesting under `<platform>/`. Without this ordering, a malicious member like `wrapper//etc/passwd` (post-wrapper: `/etc/passwd`, absolute) would have been neutralized by the platform prefix into `linux-64//etc/passwd`, which `Path()` normalizes to a non-absolute path inside dest — defeating the check. The new test `test_absolute_path_rejected_with_platform_prefix` pins this so a future refactor can't silently re-introduce the gap. The final `target.relative_to(dest)` resolved-path backstop remains belt-and-suspenders. **Test changes** in `tests/unit/test_pr_artifacts_cli.py`: `_make_fixture_zip` updated to the real Azure shape (`conda_pkgs_<job>/<file>`, no inner platform). `TestExtractZipSafety.test_clean_zip_extracts_normally` rewritten to use the real shape + pass `platform="linux-64"`. `test_dot_dot_traversal_rejected` now passes `platform="linux-64"` (the production call shape). Two new cases: `test_absolute_path_rejected_with_platform_prefix` (security regression) + `test_platforms_filter_short_circuits_whole_zip` (whole-zip filter). Suite: 54/54 pass in 0.21s. **Live re-verification**: `pixi run -e local-recipes pr-artifacts 33693` now produces `extracted/{linux-64,osx-64,win-64}/{gh-copilot-cli-*.conda,repodata.json,...}` — three proper subdir-tagged channels under one root. `mamba install -c file:///.../extracted gh-copilot-cli` resolves to the linux-64 build automatically (no explicit-path workaround needed); the smoke-tested `copilot --version` prints `GitHub Copilot CLI 1.0.61.` as before. **Manifest `extracted_to` field** (`"extracted/<platform>/"`) was already documenting this layout — it's been honest for two PATCH versions; only the implementation has caught up. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.14.2.

**v8.14.1** (Jun 12, 2026) — `pr_artifacts.download_artifact` integrity check: swap strict size match for `zipfile.ZipFile(target).testzip()`. **PATCH bump** — bug fix; no API change. **What was wrong**: v8.14.0's post-stream verification compared the on-disk byte count against Azure's `artifact["size"]` from `/_apis/build/builds/{id}/artifacts`. But that field is the artifact's logical/content size (sum of contained files), not the on-demand ZIP-stream size (which Azure generates on request and includes ZIP framing + compression overhead). They routinely diverge on valid downloads, and v8.14.0 then refused to extract a perfectly good ZIP. **Live trigger**: PR #33693 buildId 1536673 (gh-copilot-cli 1.0.61 staged-recipes submission, the same case study v8.14.0 was specced against) — `conda_pkgs_win.zip` declared 85,000,797 bytes / delivered 89,492,340 bytes, `unzip -tq` reported the archive as clean, v8.14.0 raised `RuntimeError: Size mismatch ...`. **Fix**: open the on-disk file with `zipfile.ZipFile(target)` and call `testzip()` — which CRC-validates every member by decompressing and recomputing each one against the stored CRC. `BadZipFile` on open → `RuntimeError("Corrupt ZIP for <name>: ...")`; non-None member from `testzip()` → `RuntimeError("CRC failure in <name>: member <m> is corrupt ...")`. Both preserve the `.zip` in place for forensics, matching v8.14.0's contract. Azure's stale `size` is now informational only (`entry["size_bytes"] = art["size"]` in the manifest is unchanged). **Why this is stronger, not weaker**: a truncated deflated ZIP cannot keep a valid central directory — `BadZipFile` or `testzip()` mismatch catches both truncation and bit-rot; the previous size-equality check would have *missed* a hypothetical truncation that ended on a coincidentally-correct byte count and a manipulated central-directory offset. **Test changes** in `tests/unit/test_azure_download.py`: 4 → 6 cases. `test_size_match_returns_target_path` → `test_valid_zip_returns_target_path` (body now a real minimal ZIP, asserts happy path). New `test_valid_zip_tolerates_stale_declared_size` — the bug-direct regression: declared `size: 85_000_797` against real-zip body of arbitrary length must not raise. New `test_non_zip_body_raises_and_preserves` — `BadZipFile` path. New `test_corrupt_member_raises_and_preserves` — flips a byte in the deflated payload and asserts `CRC failure` OR `Corrupt ZIP` (either is an accepted forensic path; zipfile's library can raise from either gate depending on where corruption lands). `test_missing_download_url_raises` unchanged. `test_size_none_skips_verification` → `test_size_none_still_verifies_zip` (the gate is no longer size-based, so size: None no longer bypasses verification). 6/6 pass in 0.04s; broader PR-artifacts suite (`test_pr_artifacts_cli`, `test_pr_artifacts_resolver`, `test_azure_artifacts_lister`, `test_download_pr_artifacts_mcp`) — 46/46 still pass. **Live re-verification**: `pixi run -e local-recipes pr-artifacts 33693` end-to-end after the fix downloads all 3 platform ZIPs, extracts them to a valid `file://` mamba channel. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.14.1.

**v8.14.0** (Jun 12, 2026) — New `pr-artifacts` pixi task + `pr_artifacts.py` CLI + `download_pr_artifacts` FastMCP tool for fetching CI-published `.conda` artifacts from any conda-forge staged-recipes or feedstock PR. **MINOR bump** — net-new user-facing feature; no breaking changes to existing CLIs / MCP tools / build flow. **Why it exists**: staged-recipes' Azure CI publishes `conda_pkgs_(linux|osx|win).zip` artifacts when a recipe sets `azure.store_build_artifacts: true`, but the Azure DevOps UI requires ~5 clicks per platform per PR with no batch path — killing the "review the artifact, not just the diff" loop. The v8.13.2 `recipe-build-cross` wrapper closed the inverse gap (platforms CI doesn't cover); v8.14.0 closes this one (platforms CI DID build, but the bytes are stuck behind clicks). **Mechanics**: (1) `pr_artifacts.parse_pr_ref()` accepts a bare PR number or full GitHub URL and resolves to `(repo, pr_number)`; (2) `resolve_build_ids()` invokes `gh pr checks <pr> --repo <repo> --json name,link,bucket,state`, auto-detects the `staged-recipes` row on staged-recipes repos vs `^<pkg>-feedstock$` on feedstock repos (overridable via `--check-name`), and regexes `buildId=(\d+)` out of the `link` field; `--all-runs` returns every distinct buildId descending vs default-to-highest; (3) `list_azure_artifacts()` issues a single anonymous GET against `https://dev.azure.com/conda-forge/feedstock-builds/_apis/build/builds/<id>/artifacts?api-version=7.1`, default-filters to `^conda_pkgs_(linux|osx|win)$` (override via `--all-artifacts`), and maps each artifact name to the conda-forge platform; (4) `download_artifact()` streams each ZIP via `_http.fetch_to_file_resumable` (`.part` sibling + Range/206/416 resume + atomic rename) into `build_artifacts/pr/<pr-number>/<buildId>/<name>.zip`, then verifies on-disk byte count against Azure's declared `artifactsize`; (5) `extract_zip()` flattens exactly one level (Azure ZIPs ship `conda-build_<job>/<platform>/*.conda` → `extracted/<platform>/*.conda`) producing a valid `file://` mamba channel; (6) `--keep-zips` controls cleanup (default OFF; ZIPs deleted post-extract); (7) `--platforms linux-64,osx-64` filters which extracted subdirs land; (8) per-buildId `pr-artifacts.json` manifest is the cache key — second run on a populated `<buildId>/` skips the network with `"skipped (cached)"` unless `--force`; (9) `--json` emits the full manifest summary to stdout, which the MCP tool subprocess-parses. **Anonymous Azure auth** — the public `feedstock-builds` project doesn't need a PAT, but `_http`'s existing auth chain would unconditionally inject `JFROG_API_KEY` / `GITHUB_TOKEN` cross-host. Fixed at the source: new `skip_auth: bool = False` kwarg on `auth_headers_for()` + `make_request()` + `fetch_to_file_resumable()` — when True, return empty / skip the auth merge. The pr_artifacts.py call sites pass `skip_auth=True` explicitly. A host allowlist refactor is tracked as v8.15 hardening (smaller blast radius this release; explicit opt-in at call site makes the security intent visible). **3-tier discipline**: canonical at `scripts/pr_artifacts.py`; wrapper at `.claude/scripts/conda-forge-expert/pr_artifacts.py`; pixi task `pr-artifacts` in `pixi.toml`; SCRIPTS list entry in `tests/meta/test_all_scripts_runnable.py`; `download_pr_artifacts` MCP tool in `.claude/tools/conda_forge_server.py` (subprocess via `_run_script` with `timeout=600` — multi-platform ZIPs run several minutes). **22 new unit tests** across 6 files: `test_http_skip_auth.py` (4 — JFROG/GitHub bypass + regression guard), `test_pr_artifacts_resolver.py` (12 — parse_pr_ref happy + URL variants + invalid, resolve_build_ids staged/feedstock/all-runs/highest/no-azure/explicit-name), `test_azure_artifacts_lister.py` (3 — default filter + include_all + skip_auth wiring), `test_azure_download.py` (4 — size match/mismatch/missing-url/no-size-skip), `test_pr_artifacts_cli.py` (9 — help, extract layout, keep-zips on/off, cache + force, JSON mode, no-Azure rc1, platforms filter) and `test_download_pr_artifacts_mcp.py` (4 — happy path returns manifest, non-zero exit → error key, extract=False propagates, optional flags wire correctly). `_http` regression run (85 existing tests) still green; full meta-test suite carries pre-existing baseline failures unrelated to v8.14.0. **SKILL.md** § "Submit PR" gains a v8.14.0 bullet cross-referencing `pr-artifacts` for post-monitor artifact fetch. `guides/testing-recipes.md` gains a new § "Downloading artifacts from a PR" (4-line usage + `mamba install -c file://...` example). `quickref/commands-cheatsheet.md` gains a one-line entry under the v8.13.2 "Local builds via pixi" section. `reference/mcp-tools.md` adds `download_pr_artifacts` to the Security and Maintenance tool inventory. **MCP server restart caveat** (same as v8.13.0 `_extract_json_from_stdout` fix): the new tool only becomes callable after Claude Code restarts the MCP server — the CLI works immediately, but `download_pr_artifacts` as a tool requires a restart to pick up the new `@mcp.tool()` registration. **Live case study**: the gh-copilot-cli staged-recipes#33693 session drove the spec — buildId 1536673, 3 platform artifacts (linux/osx/win); the captured `gh pr checks` JSON shape is the fixture data backing `test_pr_artifacts_resolver.py`. **Spec**: `_bmad-output/projects/local-recipes/implementation-artifacts/spec-cfe-pr-artifact-downloader-v8.14.0.md`. **Post-review hardening (13 patches, same release)**: step-04 adversarial review by three reviewers (Blind Hunter / Edge Case Hunter / Acceptance Auditor) surfaced 23 findings; the implementation absorbed 13 as patches (CRITICAL Zip Slip guard in `extract_zip` — absolute / `..` traversal members rejected before any write; HIGH `_gh_pr_checks` 60 s `timeout` + `TimeoutExpired` + `FileNotFoundError` friendly-error paths; MED Azure 200-with-error-envelope detection raises RuntimeError with the upstream `message`; MED `_read_cached_manifest` shape validation requires `{build_id, azure_url, artifacts}` keys → corrupt cache forces clean re-fetch; MED atomic manifest write via new `_write_manifest_atomic` (`.tmp` + `os.replace`); MED `--build-id <= 0` rejected at argparse; MED MCP tool passes `pr_ref` after `--` so leading-dash refs cannot be reinterpreted as flags; LOW corrupt-ZIP returns exit 2 per spec § I/O Matrix instead of 1; LOW `_check_name_matches` case-insensitive comparisons; LOW permissive substring fallback removed — unknown-shape repos now require explicit `--check-name`; LOW `--platforms` whitespace-only rejected by argparse; LOW `test_cached_buildid_skips_on_second_run` asserts `list_calls == 1` so cache-vs-network boundary is enforced). 19 new unit tests landed; suite now 139/139 passing (was 120 pre-patch). 9 findings deferred as DW-PA-1 through DW-PA-10 in `deferred-work.md` (host-allowlist refactor for v8.15 is the big one). 1 finding rejected. **No spec amendment needed**; the Intent + Boundaries blocks held. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.14.0.

**v8.13.2** (Jun 11, 2026) — New `recipe-build-cross` pixi task + `.claude/scripts/conda-forge-expert/cross-build.sh` wrapper for producing downloadable `.conda` artifacts on platforms staged-recipes' Azure CI doesn't build at PR time (`osx-arm64`, `linux-aarch64`). **PATCH bump** — additive: one new script + one pixi task + one guide section + one quickref entry; no behavior change for existing flows. **Why it exists**: staged-recipes' Azure pipeline matrix is hardcoded to `linux_64` / `osx_64` / `win_64` (see `.azure-pipelines/azure-pipelines-osx.yml` upstream — `osx_arm64` is not in the matrix). Reviewers asking for an `osx-arm64` smoke test before merge currently had no path: native-build.sh only targets the host platform, and per-recipe `conda-forge.yml` overrides can't expand the staged-recipes matrix (it's regenerated from the staged-recipes root config, not per-recipe). The wrapper produces a `.conda` you can ship to a real target-platform machine, install with `mamba install -c local <path>.conda`, and smoke-test before the post-merge feedstock CI publishes the official build. **Mechanics**: (1) loads `.ci_support/<config>.yaml` + `conda-forge-pinning` overlay so variant resolution mirrors upstream CI; (2) sets `CONDA_OVERRIDE_OSX` / `CONDA_OVERRIDE_GLIBC` so the host virtual-package solve succeeds on a cross host (the `__osx >=11.0` / `__glibc >=2.17` host spec otherwise can't resolve on a foreign-arch host); (3) for osx-arm64 / osx-64 cross builds: copies the recipe to a tempdir and (a) injects `cctools_<arch>` + `ld64_<arch>` into `requirements.build` via a single-output regex against the top-level `requirements.build:` block, (b) appends a 6-line shim to `build.sh` that symlinks the `<triple>-install_name_tool` cross-tool to the plain `install_name_tool` name rattler-build's Mach-O relinker searches for; (4) for win-64 cross: overrides `build.script: bash ./build.sh` in the recipe so rattler-build uses bash instead of trying to spawn `build.bat` under absent-on-unix cmd.exe — the recipe's `build.sh` MUST handle `target_platform == "win-64"` itself (write to `${PREFIX}/Library/bin` with `.exe` suffix); (5) passes `--test skip` because rattler-build can't execute foreign-arch binaries on the host. **Scope**: tuned for binary-repackage recipes (the staged-recipes pattern for prebuilt CLI tools like `gh-copilot-cli`, `pixi`, `microsoft-edit`). Compiled-source cross-builds need more wiring (sysroot, kernel-headers, compiler shims) that this wrapper doesn't set up — for those, build natively or use the Docker entrypoint. **Single-output only**: the cctools-injection regex matches one top-level `requirements.build:` block; multi-output recipes should edit their own build deps and use `rattler-build build` directly. **Subtle regex gotcha discovered during implementation**: the cctools-injection regex originally used `(?ms)` for MULTILINE + DOTALL, which made `.` match newlines and greedily swallowed the entire file past the `build:` block, capturing `tests:`, `about:`, `extra:` into the substitution target. Fixed by dropping DOTALL — `(?m)` only — so the trailing `(?:    .*\n)+` correctly terminates at the first blank line / non-4-space-indented line. **Live case study**: gh-copilot-cli 1.0.61 staged-recipes#33693 needed an osx-arm64 artifact for reviewer smoke-testing. Cross-built from linux-64 via the wrapper; 78 MiB `.conda` at `build_artifacts/osxarm64/osx-arm64/gh-copilot-cli-1.0.61-h56b3cad_0.conda` in ~10 seconds wall-clock (cache-warm). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.13.2.

**v8.13.1** (Jun 11, 2026) — Gotcha **G17** lands from the `recipes/open-design` v0.2.0 → v0.9.0 bump session. **PATCH bump** — additive: one new SKILL.md gotcha section + this CHANGELOG entry; no code, test, or template changes. `pnpm install --ignore-scripts` only suppresses *dependency* install scripts; the root project's own `pre*` / `post*` lifecycle scripts run regardless. Fix: strip the root `postinstall` from `package.json` before `pnpm install` via a 4-line Python `json` snippet (idempotent across version bumps; survives upstream restructure without a `patches/<name>.patch` to re-roll). Live case study: the open-design recipe was committed at v0.2.0 with a `--ignore-scripts` flag + a comment claiming it skipped root postinstall — the comment was empirically false, the recipe had never actually been built. Bumping to v0.9.0 surfaced the bug when upstream's `scripts/postinstall.mjs` `buildTargets` list grew from 4 entries to 13 (adding `packages/download`, `packages/host`, `packages/registry-protocol`, `packages/agui-adapter`, `packages/plugin-runtime`, `packages/diagnostics`, `tools/dev`, `tools/pack`, `tools/serve`). The newly-added `packages/download` workspace's build needed `esbuild` which the daemon-filter install didn't fetch. Patch fixed by stripping `postinstall` from `package.json` before `pnpm install`. The fix applies broadly to any Node-monorepo recipe using a `--filter '@org/<app>...'` install of a sibling workspace whose upstream has a workspace-root `postinstall` that builds packages outside the filter chain. Same root-vs-dependency distinction applies to `preinstall` / `prepare` / `prepublish` lifecycle scripts — audit `package.json scripts:` for anything in-install-scope. Bonus finding from the same session: the optimizer (`optimize_recipe`) returned `[]` against `recipes/open-design/recipe.yaml` v0.2.0 — zero v8.13.0 check codes flagged, confirming the schema-header + license-file-list + maintainer + stdlib-for-compiled patterns the May 2 author chose have held. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.13.1.

**v8.13.0** (Jun 11, 2026) — Generator-hardening sprint closes the accumulated S1+S3 retro backlog + the 2026-06-11 operator `python_min` enforcement correction. **MINOR bump** — additive: 3 new grayskull post-processors + 1 wrapper fix + 1 SKILL.md gotcha (G16) + 2 SKILL.md notes (post-edit rebuild discipline §8b; retro→spec feed-forward) + 1 doc correction (R1: `edit_recipe` `add` action removed from tool table) + 19 new unit tests. Wave A of the 3-wave sprint specced at `_bmad-output/projects/local-recipes/implementation-artifacts/spec-cfe-generator-hardening-v8.13.0.md`; Wave B (new optimizer checks ABT-003 + SEL-004 + meta-test) and Wave C (60-recipe drift sweep) follow in the same session. **Three new grayskull post-processors in `conda_forge_server.py`:** (1) **`_clamp_or_drop_context_python_min`** — closes C1 (S1 retro) + 2026-06-11 operator correction. Reads conda-forge floor dynamically from `.pixi/envs/local-recipes/conda_build_config.yaml` (no hardcode — floor moves; falls back to `"3.10"` if read fails). Drops the `context.python_min:` line when value ≤ floor (redundant or below-floor); keeps when value > floor (legitimate override). `${{ python_min }}` references resolve from `conda-forge-pinning` at build time. Per SKILL.md § Python Version Policy item 6. (2) **`_add_missing_description`** — closes C2 (S1 retro). Parallels v8.12.0's `_add_missing_repository`. Pulls `info.description` from PyPI JSON (or caller-passed dict to avoid duplicate fetch); skips if already present in recipe, equal to summary, or too short (<20 chars stripped). Inserts as `description: |` block scalar after `summary:` line; first paragraph only; capped at 500 chars to avoid embedding full READMEs. (3) **`_strip_grayskull_placeholders`** — closes C3 (S3 retro). Three pattern families: (a) `summary: "Add your description here"` (and `uv init` / `rye init` / `hatch init` defaults) → prepends `# TODO: review — grayskull placeholder` recipe-comment marker above the line (preserves value, surfaces to operator); (b) empty `license:` + PyPI classifier maps to recognised SPDX → substitutes the SPDX value (`License :: OSI Approved :: MIT License` → `MIT`, etc.; 7-entry classifier→SPDX map); (c) `license_file: PLEASE_ADD_LICENSE_FILE` (and `PLEASE_ADD_LICENSE` / `TODO` / `FIXME`) → prepends `# TODO: vendor LICENSE per SKILL.md pattern (2)` marker. All three patterns are idempotent. **JSON-extraction helper `_extract_json_from_stdout`** — closes C4 (S3 retro). Replaces the direct `json.loads(result.stdout)` in `_run_script` with a two-pass extractor: try direct parse first; on failure, regex for the first `{`/`[` at the start of a line and parse from there. Fixes the cosmetic-but-misleading `error: "Failed to parse JSON output"` that fired on every `prepare_submission_branch` / `submit_pr` call because those scripts emit `"  Syncing fork with upstream conda-forge/staged-recipes ..."` as a progress line before the JSON body. **Note: takes effect on next MCP server restart** — the `conda_forge_server.py` module is imported once at MCP server boot; the running interpreter doesn't re-read the file on disk. If `prepare_submission_branch` / `submit_pr` still return the cosmetic error after v8.13.0 lands, the server process pre-dates the fix; restart Claude Code (which respawns the MCP server) to pick it up. The inner CLI scripts are correct independent of the server state — the branch lands / PR opens despite the wrapper error; only the structured result is malformed. **`generate_recipe_from_pypi` MCP response gains three new `post_processing:` keys**: `context_python_min_dropped`, `about_description_added`, `grayskull_placeholders_stripped` — each `bool`, parallel to existing post-processor fields. PyPI JSON is fetched once per generation now and shared between `_add_missing_description` + `_strip_grayskull_placeholders` (was twice in the design draft — single-fetch optimisation). **R1 — `edit_recipe` tool-table correction**: SKILL.md v8.11.1 added `add` to the supported actions list after `remove` was found broken; empirical retest during the v8.13.0 sprint showed `add` returns `Unknown action type: add` (verified at `recipe_editor.py:113-145` — only `update`, `add_to_list`, `remove_from_list`, `calculate_hash` exist). However: `update` uses `setdefault` for intermediate keys + plain dict assignment at the leaf, so it ALSO handles inserting new keys (S1+S3 hit this confusion). Corrected the tool-table entry to enumerate the 4 real actions + clarify `update` covers both modify AND insert + direct `Edit` fallback for deletions OR multi-line block-scalar inserts. **Two new SKILL.md notes** at the §8b "Prepare Submission Branch" section + § Sub-workflow ("Updating an existing recipe"): (a) post-edit rebuild discipline — if the recipe was edited after a green build, re-run `trigger_build` before `prepare_submission_branch` (same-package extension of G15; the fork should always reflect a verified-green state); (b) retro→spec feed-forward — when a recent retro entry exists, pre-apply its known-gaps workarounds as Execution checklist items in the new spec (verified pattern from S3's spec consuming S1's retro). **New gotcha G16: PyPI Varnish CDN degradation on `/packages/source/<letter>/...` route** — symptom (rattler-build 503 from `pypi.org/packages/source/...` while `files.pythonhosted.org/packages/<hash>/...` returns 200), why (Varnish edge layer routing issue; backing CDN keeps serving), workaround (URL-swap to `files.pythonhosted.org` form for local build only — sha256 unchanged — REVERT before pushing fork; re-validate post-revert), risk (forgetting to revert leaves a non-canonical URL that bypasses JFrog Artifactory proxies), detection (dual `curl -sI` probe), case study (S3 lyric-task 0.1.7, 2026-06-11, >12 min). **19 new unit tests in `tests/unit/test_grayskull_post_processors.py`**: `TestExtractJsonFromStdout` (5 cases — direct, prefixed, indented, no-json-raises, array), `TestReadCondaForgePythonFloor` (1 case — default-on-missing), `TestClampOrDropContextPythonMin` (5 cases — drops at floor, drops below floor at 3.9 + 3.8, keeps above floor, no-op when absent), `TestAddMissingDescription` (5 cases — inserts, skips-already-present, skips-equal-to-summary, skips-too-short, skips-no-info), `TestStripGrayskullPlaceholders` (4 cases — marks placeholder summary, infers license from classifier, marks license_file placeholder, no-op on clean recipe). Test pattern follows v8.12.0 convention: `importlib` + stubbed `fastmcp` module + `tmp_path` fixtures + direct function calls on the loaded `cfs` module + assertions on output text. Suite: 30/30 passing in 0.07s. **Wave B + Wave C land in the same session under the same v8.13.0 release** — see CHANGELOG entries that follow when written (or look at the spec). Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.13.0.

**v8.12.2** (Jun 11, 2026) — Documentation-only PATCH bump from the S3 lyric-task retro under BMAD-quick-dev. **C1 + C2 + R1 from S1's v8.12.1 retro REPRODUCED** exactly as predicted; pre-applied workarounds in S3's spec shipped clean — validates the retro→deferred-work→next-spec feed-forward loop (refinement R2 below). **Three new findings:** (1) **C3 — grayskull placeholder literals shipped unflagged**. For PyPI packages with empty/placeholder pyproject metadata (`description = "Add your description here"` — the default `uv init` / `rye init` / `hatch init` placeholder), grayskull emits the placeholder directly into `about.summary`. Same for empty PyPI `license` field (emitted as bare `license:` with no value) and grayskull's `"PLEASE_ADD_LICENSE_FILE"` literal in `about.license_file`. `optimize_recipe` doesn't flag any of these today; conda-forge reviewer would reject the PR on the first one. Fix shape: new `ABT-003 ("placeholder-shaped about-field")` optimizer check matching common placeholder patterns + empty/missing `license:` + `"PLEASE_ADD_*"` strings; optionally pair with `_strip_grayskull_placeholders` post-processor in `conda_forge_server.py`. (2) **C4 — `prepare_submission_branch` MCP wrapper JSON-parse cosmetic error**. Wrapper returns `error: "Failed to parse JSON output"` despite the inner CLI's valid JSON. Inner stdout shows `success: true, pushed: true, head_sha: ...`. Cause: wrapper doesn't strip the prefix line `"  Syncing fork with upstream conda-forge/staged-recipes ..."` from stdout before `json.loads()`. One-line fix. (3) **A1 — new gotcha G16: PyPI Varnish CDN degradation on `/packages/source/<letter>/...` route**. Symptom: rattler-build's source fetch returns 503 from `pypi.org/packages/source/...` while `files.pythonhosted.org/packages/<hash>/...` returns 200 (identical bytes). Observed sustained >12 min on 2026-06-11 for `lyric-task` 0.1.7 build. Workaround applied: temporarily edit `source.url` to the backing CDN form, verify sha256, build green, revert URL to canonical before pushing fork. **Risk**: forgetting to revert leaves the recipe with a non-canonical URL that bypasses JFrog Artifactory PyPI Remote Repository proxies (SKILL.md "PyPI source.url Must Use..." critical constraint). Worth landing as gotcha G16 in SKILL.md. (4) **R2 — retro→spec feed-forward pattern verified**. S3's spec authored 2026-06-11 explicitly referenced the S1 retro via `context:` frontmatter and pre-applied C1+C2+R1 workarounds in the Execution checklist. Result: zero step-04 PATCH iterations; all known gaps shipped clean. Worth a short note under § Sub-workflow ("Updating an existing recipe") that new recipe specs should pre-apply the most recent retro's known-gaps as Execution items, not assume the skill has been patched. (5) **A2 — SKILL.md "Canonical License-File Placement" pattern (2) verified end-to-end**. Sdist had no LICENSE; vendored MIT from `lyric-project/lyric-runtime` into `recipes/lyric-task/LICENSE`; recipe references `license_file: [LICENSE]`; rattler-build resolved relative to recipe directory; build green. Successful precedent for S5/S6/S7 (lyric-* workers — same upstream LICENSE source, same sdist-missing pattern). (6) **Verified existing guidance held**: SKILL.md pattern (2) License-File Placement (A2), `feedback_loosen_pins.md` for the `hatchling==1.26.3` exact pin, `feedback_pypi_conda_mapping_unreliable.md` four-form check (grayskull DID resolve `msgpack`→`msgpack-python` automatically — four-form check is still right discipline for unknowns but didn't fire here), CLAUDE.md Rule 1, CFE-canonical branch name (`add-recipe-lyric-task`), two-step submission flow (operator chose [H] Hold; respected). (7) **No new cross-skill findings** — `feedback_bmad_cfe_branch_name_convention.md` (from S1) continues to apply. (8) **No SKILL.md edits this bump** — C3/C4/A1/R2/A2 land as code fixes (C3, C4) or doc additions (A1, R2) deferred to the next generator-hardening sprint. **v8.12.1** (Jun 10, 2026) — Documentation-only PATCH bump from the S1 abstract-singleton retro under BMAD-quick-dev. Two real generator gaps surfaced + documented; fixes deferred to a follow-up effort (S1 OOS-4: don't touch skill scripts during recipe-authoring effort). (1) **`context.python_min` clamp gap** — `_resolve_python_min()` exists at `recipe-generator.py:213` and correctly clamps via `max(detected, conda_forge_floor)`, but the grayskull-PyPI path in `conda_forge_server.py` does NOT invoke it. v8.12.0's `_clamp_run_python_floor` closed the parallel `requirements.run` echo gap but not the `context.python_min` emission gap. **Live reproducer**: `generate_recipe_from_pypi(package_name="abstract-singleton", version="1.0.1")` emitted `context.python_min: "3.9"` against upstream's `requires-python = ">=3.8"`. Reproducible for any noarch:python sdist with `requires-python = ">=3.X"` where X<10. Fix shape: `_clamp_context_python_min` post-processor mirroring `_clamp_run_python_floor`'s text-replacement pattern + unit tests for `>=3.8` / `>=3.9` / `>=3.10` / `>=3.11`. PackageInfo carries `description` (line 83 + 1170) populated from PyPI's `info.description` (line 757), but the grayskull-PyPI path never inserts it — only the npm path consumes it (line 1627-1664). **Live reproducer**: `abstract-singleton` recipe had no `about.description`; both step-04 reviewers flagged it; patched via direct `Edit` (then `edit_recipe` `add` action returned `Unknown action type: add` — see refinement R1 below). Fix shape: `_add_missing_description` paralleling `_add_missing_repository`; source priority `info.description` → `info.summary` (only when description empty or matches summary verbatim, to avoid noise duplication). (3) **Refinement R1 — `edit_recipe` `add` action support**: SKILL.md v8.11.1 corrected the tool table to claim only `update` + `add` work (`remove` doesn't); empirical test in this effort showed `add` also fails on `about.description`. Need to verify whether `add` works on any path or whether the v8.11.1 doc correction was over-confident. (4) **Addition A1 — single-recipe stale-artifact note**: G15 covers cross-package stale-repodata; this effort surfaced the same-package case (recipe edited after green build → fork branch reflects pre-edit verification). Mitigation: rebuild after any post-build `edit_recipe` / `Edit` and before re-pushing the fork. Worth a one-line note under §8b. **v8.12.0** (Jun 10, 2026) — Two new optimizer checks (**LIC-001**, **FMT-001**) + five grayskull post-processors (items 4, 5, 6, 8, 9 from the microsoft-agents-m365copilot retro). **MINOR bump** — additive: 17 unit tests, 0 regressions on the existing 608. (1) **LIC-001 in `recipe_optimizer.py`** — flags pattern-(3) secondary-source LICENSE (e.g. `source[1].url: .../LICENSE`) and suggests pattern (2) (in-recipe LICENSE alongside `recipe.yaml`). The skill's `Canonical License-File Placement` section had said "convert to pattern (2) when you encounter it" since v8.x but no automated check enforced it; this closes the gap. Skipped on single-URL `source:` blocks. (2) **FMT-001 in `recipe_optimizer.py`** — flags YAML list items indented at the same depth as their parent mapping key (non-canonical; reviewer-flagged). Done as raw-text regex parsing because `ruamel.yaml`'s load step normalizes indent before the AST exists. Top-level lists at zero indent are excluded (stylistic). (3) **`_normalize_grayskull_test_matrix` 1-line indent fix** in `conda_forge_server.py` — the post-processor was emitting `python_version:` list items at parent-key depth (i.e. the FMT-001 bug, baked into the generator). Now emits canonical 2-spaces-deeper. (4) **`_strip_belt_and_suspenders_host`** — when grayskull emits both a PEP-517 backend (poetry-core / hatchling / flit-core / pdm-backend / scikit-build-core / maturin / meson-python) and the legacy `wheel` + `setuptools >=42.0.0` pair in `host:`, the pair is redundant. Strips them. Keeps `setuptools` when no PEP-517 backend is declared (genuine setuptools backend). G8 case study from v8.3.0 was documented but never automated — this closes the loop. (5) **`_clamp_run_python_floor`** — rewrites `- python >=3.X,<4.0` (X<10) in run to `- python >=${{ python_min }}` (when context declares python_min) or literal `- python >=3.10` (default conda-forge floor). Closes the v8.8.0 `_resolve_python_min()` regression where grayskull's `python >=3.9,<4.0` echo bypassed the clamp. (6) **`_normalize_summary`** — strips trailing parenthetical version tags from `about.summary` (e.g. `"Foo SDK (V1.0)"` → `"Foo SDK"`) and drops grayskull's stray `# readme` placeholder comments. Both are pure-cosmetic grayskull noise reviewers consistently flag. (7) **`_add_missing_repository`** — fetches PyPI's `project_urls` JSON and inserts `about.repository:` after `about.homepage:` when grayskull dropped it. Idempotent; network-bound; silently no-ops on network failure. Recognizes Repository / Source / Source Code / Code / GitHub / source keys per the v8.8.0 `_extract_project_urls` list. (8) **17 new unit tests** — 2 LIC-001/FMT-001 cases in `test_recipe_optimizer.py`; 11 cases in new `test_grayskull_post_processors.py` covering each post-processor + idempotency + the keep-setuptools-when-no-pep517 edge case. Post-processor tests use `importlib` + a stubbed `fastmcp` module to load `conda_forge_server.py` without binding the MCP server. (9) **Known gap — pre-release pin clamp (item 7)** deferred: when grayskull emits `microsoft-agents-m365copilot-core >=1.0.0rc1` and conda-forge ships stable `1.0.0`, the optimal recipe pins to `>=1.0.0`. Implementing this requires a conda-forge channel lookup (does a stable ≥ floor exist?) which adds network dependency to the post-processor chain. Deferred to a follow-up bump. (10) **SKILL.md `Core Tools Reference`** `edit_recipe` row corrected — claimed `remove` action existed; tool actually returns `Unknown action type: remove`. Doc now lists only `update` + `add`; deletions fall back to direct `Edit`. Discovered mid-session when removing `context.python_min` from `recipes/microsoft-agents-m365copilot/recipe.yaml`. (11) **Verified existing guidance held during the retro**: v8.11.7 diff-before-apply sub-workflow caught all 9 hunks of grayskull regression vs. canonical and let the user reject them in one prompt; v8.11.7 LICENSE pattern-(2) guidance was correct but the optimizer needed teeth (now LIC-001); v8.11.7 G15 trap (stale repodata after rebuild) did not surface because no downstream depended on the rebuilt artifact. Updated `config/skill-config.yaml` to 8.12.0.

**v8.11.8** (Jun 9, 2026) — Gotcha **G15** lands: rebuilding the same recipe locally re-hashes the `.conda` artifact (embedded timestamps) but leaves `repodata.json` stale → downstream builds fail with `hash mismatch when extracting file://...`. Fix: delete the on-disk artifact and rebuild atomically (rattler-build updates both on a fresh build vs. an idempotent re-run). PATCH bump — also adds (a) Build Failure Protocol § "Diagnostic chain for feedstock CI test failures" codifying the gh-log → upstream-pyproject → feedstock-state → python-pin diagnosis chain; (b) three new special-case categorizations in the v8.11.7 diff-before-apply sub-workflow (missing test `python` pin → always a correction; upstream-explicit `requires-python` upper bound → tighten; cross-package run-dep lower-bound bumps → check prerequisite feedstock state). Live case study: `conda-forge/ag-ui-langgraph-feedstock` PR #22 fix (root cause `ag-ui-a2ui-toolkit>=0.0.2` vs upstream `>=0.0.3`).

**v8.11.7** (Jun 9, 2026) — New **diff-before-apply sub-workflow** for updating an existing recipe + one-line **feedstock-vs-staged-recipes branching note** in step 9. **PATCH bump** — additive: two SKILL.md sections + CHANGELOG entry; no code change. Driven by the `conda-forge/weasyprint-feedstock` v67.0 → v69.0 local update session. Documents the move-aside + fresh-generate + enrich + diff + selective-apply pattern that surfaced grayskull dropping critical hand-curated content (`pango`, `glib` C-FFI deps + the documented workaround comment for feedstock issue #23), with a 3-bucket categorization (corrections to apply / regressions to reject / stylistic). **v8.11.6** (Jun 8, 2026) — Gotcha **G14** lands: autotick bot v0 version bumps can fail the conda-forge-linter `package.version` float-parse rule. The bot updates `{% set version = "X.Y" %}` (jinja-quoted) but `version: {{ version }}` renders as bare `X.Y`, which YAML parses as float. Fix: quote at the YAML level, or migrate v0 → v1 (v1 sidesteps the issue by construction). Live case study: feedstock PR #8 on `conda-forge/wagtail-ab-testing-feedstock`. CHANGELOG also flags the `migrate_to_v1` MCP wrapper bug (passes path as feedstock name → 404).

**v8.11.5** (Jun 7, 2026) — Gotcha **G13** lands: rattler-build's script-list entries share CWD across entries (env vars don't, per G1, but CWD does), and on Windows cmd.exe `(cmd1 && cmd2)` is command grouping, **not a subshell** — naive bash subshell patterns leak CWD into the next entry. Cross-platform fix: pushd/popd works identically in bash and cmd. Discovered live on solvor PR #33647 buildId 1534140 win_64. PATCH bump; also adds a one-line refinement to G1 cross-linking the CWD-persists caveat. CHANGELOG flags two CHANGELOG-only observations (v8.9.0 maturin auto-detection regression on solvor + grafeo; `cargo-bundle-licenses` lacks `--manifest-path`).

The G10 lookup checklist now covers bare PyPI name, hyphen↔underscore swap, `-py` suffix, AND `-python` suffix.
